python
# app/modules/delivery/repository.py
# ... (imports: ObjectId, logger, UpdateResult, BaseRepository, models, etc) ...
from .models import DeliveryInDB, DeliveryCreateInternal, DeliveryUpdateInternal, TrackingEvent, ChatMessage, GeoPoint

class DeliveryRepository(BaseRepository[DeliveryInDB, DeliveryCreateInternal, DeliveryUpdateInternal]):
    # ... (existing create_indexes, get_by_ref, list methods) ...

    async def add_tracking_event(
        self,
        delivery_id: ObjectId,
        event: TrackingEvent
        ) -> bool:
        """Adds a tracking event and potentially updates last_known_location."""
        log = logger.bind(delivery_id=str(delivery_id), event_status=event.status)
        log.debug("Adding tracking event...")
        try:
            event_dict = event.model_dump(mode='json', exclude_none=True)
            update_payload = {
                "$push": {
                    "tracking_history": {
                        "$each": [event_dict],
                        "$position": 0,
                        "$slice": 50 # Limit history size
                    }
                },
                "$set": {"updated_at": datetime.utcnow()}
            }
            # Update last_known_location IF the event has location data
            if event.location:
                 update_payload["$set"]["last_known_location"] = event.location.model_dump()

            result: UpdateResult = await self.collection.update_one(
                {"_id": delivery_id},
                update_payload
            )
            success = result.modified_count > 0
            if success: log.info("Tracking event added successfully.")
            else: log.warning("Failed to add tracking event (delivery not found?).")
            return success
        except Exception as e:
            self._handle_db_exception(e, "add_tracking_event", delivery_id)
            return False

    async def add_chat_message(
        self,
        delivery_id: ObjectId,
        message: ChatMessage
        ) -> bool:
        """Adds a chat message to the delivery's chat history."""
        log = logger.bind(delivery_id=str(delivery_id), sender=message.sender_role)
        log.debug("Adding chat message...")
        try:
            message_dict = message.model_dump(mode='json', exclude_none=True)
            result: UpdateResult = await self.collection.update_one(
                {"_id": delivery_id},
                {
                    "$push": {
                        "chat_history": {
                             "$each": [message_dict],
                             # "$position": 0, # Add to end usually for chat
                             "$slice": -100 # Keep last 100 messages
                         }
                    },
                    "$set": {"updated_at": datetime.utcnow()} # Also update main timestamp
                }
            )
            success = result.modified_count > 0
            if success: log.info("Chat message added successfully.")
            else: log.warning("Failed to add chat message (delivery not found?).")
            return success
        except Exception as e:
            self._handle_db_exception(e, "add_chat_message", delivery_id)
            return False

python
# app/modules/delivery/services.py
# ... (imports: Optional, List, Dict, Any, datetime, ObjectId, HTTPException, status, logger, etc) ...
from .repository import DeliveryRepository
from .models import (
    DeliveryInDB, DeliveryCreateInternal, TrackingEvent, ChatMessage, GeoPoint, SENDER_ROLES,
    DeliveryAPI, TrackingEventAPI, ChatMessageAPI, DeliveryLocationAPI # API Models
)
from app.modules.sales.models import OrderInDB # Need Order model
from app.core.counters import CounterService
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository
from app.modules.people.models import UserInDB
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService
from app.websocket.connection_manager import manager as ws_manager # For push notifications

# --- Utility Function ---
def generate_map_link(lat: float, lon: float) -> str:
    return f"https://maps.google.com/?q={lat},{lon}"


class DeliveryService:
    # ... (existing _enrich_delivery - needs update to include location/chat if needed in main API response) ...

    async def create_delivery_from_order( # Renamed from create_tracking_thread
        self,
        order: OrderInDB, # Receive the order object directly
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository,
        counter_service: CounterService,
        # audit_service: AuditService, # Called by OrderService/Router
        # current_user: UserInDB # System action?
    ) -> DeliveryInDB:
        log = logger.bind(order_id=str(order.id), service="DeliveryService")
        log.info("Service: Creating delivery record from confirmed order...")

        # 1. Check if delivery already exists for this order
        existing_delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_order_id(order.id)
        if existing_delivery:
            log.warning(f"Delivery already exists for order {order.order_ref}.")
            # Return existing or raise error? Raise for clarity if called inappropriately.
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT,
                detail=f"Delivery already exists for order {order.order_ref}"
            )

        # 2. Check order address
        if not order.shipping_address or not order.shipping_address.get("street"):
             raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail="Order is missing a valid shipping address")

        # 3. Generate Reference
        try:
            delivery_ref = await counter_service.generate_reference("DLV")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Could not generate delivery reference: {e}")

        # 4. Prepare internal data (includes initial tracking event and empty chat history)
        delivery_internal_data = DeliveryCreateInternal(
            delivery_ref=delivery_ref,
            order_id=order.id,
            customer_id=order.customer_id,
            delivery_address=order.shipping_address,
            current_status="pending",
            shipping_notes=getattr(order, 'shipping_notes', None),
            # estimated_delivery_date=... # Add logic if needed
            # tracking_history default creates pending event
            # chat_history default creates empty list
        )

        # 5. Create using the repository
        try:
            created_delivery_db = await delivery_repo.create(delivery_internal_data)
            log.success(f"Delivery {delivery_ref} created successfully for order {order.order_ref}.")
            # Note: OrderService should handle updating the order with the delivery_id
            return created_delivery_db
        except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
             log.error(f"Failed to create delivery in DB: {e}")
             raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Could not save delivery record: {e}")

    async def add_chat_message_service(
        self,
        delivery_id_str: str,
        message_text: str,
        sender_role: SENDER_ROLES,
        sender_id: str, # User ID (customer/driver) or 'system'
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository,
        user_repo: UserRepository, # To enrich sender name
        audit_service: Optional[AuditService] = None, # Optional
        current_user: Optional[UserInDB] = None # For audit
    ) -> ChatMessageAPI:
        log = logger.bind(delivery_id=delivery_id_str, sender_role=sender_role, sender_id=sender_id)
        log.info("Service: Adding chat message...")

        delivery_id = delivery_repo._to_objectid(delivery_id_str)
        if not delivery_id: raise HTTPException(400, "Invalid Delivery ID")

        # Basic validation
        if not message_text.strip(): raise HTTPException(400, "Message cannot be empty")

        # Create internal ChatMessage model
        chat_message = ChatMessage(
            sender_role=sender_role,
            sender_id=sender_id,
            message=message_text.strip()
        )

        # Add to repository
        success = await delivery_repo.add_chat_message(delivery_id, chat_message)
        if not success:
            # Check if delivery exists before raising 500
            if not await delivery_repo.exists({"_id": delivery_id}):
                raise HTTPException(404, "Delivery not found")
            log.error("Failed to add chat message to repository.")
            raise HTTPException(500, "Failed to save chat message.")

        log.success("Chat message added to delivery.")

        # Enrich for API response and WebSocket broadcast
        sender_name = sender_id # Default
        if sender_role != 'system':
            user = await user_repo.get_by_id(sender_id)
            if user and user.profile:
                 sender_name = f"{user.profile.first_name or ''} {user.profile.last_name or ''}".strip() or user.email

        chat_api = ChatMessageAPI(
            message_id=chat_message.message_id,
            sender_role=chat_message.sender_role,
            sender_id=chat_message.sender_id,
            sender_display_name=sender_name,
            message=chat_message.message,
            timestamp=chat_message.timestamp
        )

        # Emit WebSocket event
        ws_payload = {
            "type": "new_delivery_message",
            "payload": {
                "delivery_id": delivery_id_str,
                "chat_message": chat_api.model_dump(mode='json')
            }
        }
        # Determine recipients (customer, driver, maybe admin?)
        # Fetch delivery to get customer/driver IDs
        delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id)
        if delivery:
             recipients = {str(delivery.customer_id)}
             if delivery.assigned_driver_id:
                 recipients.add(str(delivery.assigned_driver_id))
             # Send to specific users involved
             for user_id_to_notify in recipients:
                 # Don't send back to the sender? Optional.
                 # if user_id_to_notify != sender_id:
                     try:
                         await ws_manager.send_personal_message(ws_payload, user_id_to_notify)
                         log.debug(f"Sent WS delivery message notification to user {user_id_to_notify}")
                     except Exception as ws_err:
                         log.error(f"Failed to send WS message to user {user_id_to_notify}: {ws_err}")
             # Or broadcast to all staff? Depends on requirements.
             # await ws_manager.broadcast(ws_payload)

        # Audit log (optional)
        if audit_service and current_user:
            await audit_service.log_audit_event(
                 action="delivery_chat_message_sent", status="success", entity_type="Delivery",
                 entity_id=delivery_id, audit_repo=None,
                 details={"sender": sender_role, "preview": message_text[:50]},
                 current_user=current_user, request=None
             )

        return chat_api

    async def get_tracking_history(
        self,
        delivery_id_str: str,
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository
    ) -> List[TrackingEventAPI]:
        delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id_str)
        if not delivery: raise HTTPException(404, "Delivery not found")
        # Convert internal model list to API model list
        return [TrackingEventAPI.model_validate(event) for event in delivery.tracking_history]

    async def get_last_location(
        self,
        delivery_id_str: str,
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository
    ) -> DeliveryLocationAPI:
        delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id_str)
        if not delivery: raise HTTPException(404, "Delivery not found")

        location_api = DeliveryLocationAPI(address_description=delivery.delivery_address.get("street", "N/A")) # Default to street addr
        if delivery.last_known_location:
            location_api.latitude = delivery.last_known_location.latitude
            location_api.longitude = delivery.last_known_location.longitude
            location_api.map_link = generate_map_link(location_api.latitude, location_api.longitude)
            # Find the timestamp of the last location update in tracking history
            last_loc_event = next((e for e in delivery.tracking_history if e.location), None)
            location_api.last_update = last_loc_event.timestamp if last_loc_event else delivery.updated_at

        return location_api

    async def get_chat_history(
        self,
        delivery_id_str: str,
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository,
        user_repo: UserRepository, # For enrichment
    ) -> List[ChatMessageAPI]:
        delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id_str)
        if not delivery: raise HTTPException(404, "Delivery not found")

        # Enrich sender names
        enriched_chat = []
        user_cache = {} # Simple cache for user lookups within this request
        for msg in delivery.chat_history:
            sender_name = msg.sender_id
            if msg.sender_role != 'system' and msg.sender_id not in user_cache:
                 user = await user_repo.get_by_id(msg.sender_id)
                 user_cache[msg.sender_id] = user
                 if user and user.profile:
                     sender_name = f"{user.profile.first_name or ''} {user.profile.last_name or ''}".strip() or user.email
            elif msg.sender_id in user_cache:
                 user = user_cache[msg.sender_id]
                 if user and user.profile:
                     sender_name = f"{user.profile.first_name or ''} {user.profile.last_name or ''}".strip() or user.email

            enriched_chat.append(ChatMessageAPI(
                message_id=msg.message_id,
                sender_role=msg.sender_role,
                sender_id=msg.sender_id, # Keep original ID
                sender_display_name=sender_name,
                message=msg.message,
                timestamp=msg.timestamp
            ))
        return enriched_chat

    # --- TODO: Fallback Logic ---
    # This needs a Celery Task scheduled periodically or triggered by events
    async def check_location_fallback(self, delivery_id: ObjectId, time_threshold_minutes: int = 30):
        # 1. Fetch delivery
        # 2. Check timestamp of last tracking event with location data
        # 3. If older than threshold:
        #    a. Log warning / Increment internal counter?
        #    b. Generate estimated arrival time (complex)
        #    c. Send internal notification (WebSocket hint to staff?)
        #    d. Potentially send message to customer/driver via add_chat_message_service (role='system')
        #    e. Trigger 'call driver' button visibility via WebSocket hint?
        pass

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/sales/services.py (Modify create_order)**

python
# app/modules/sales/services.py
# ... (imports: OrderInDB, OrderCreateAPI, OrderRepository, etc...) ...
from app.modules.delivery.services import DeliveryService, get_delivery_service # <<< Import DeliveryService
from app.modules.delivery.repository import DeliveryRepository, get_delivery_repository # <<< Import DeliveryRepo

class OrderService:
    # ... (_select_price_tier, _process_order_items, _validate_customer) ...

    async def create_order(
        self,
        order_in: OrderCreateAPI,
        creator: UserInDB,
        order_repo: OrderRepository,
        product_repo: ProductRepository,
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        counter_service: CounterService,
        reservation_service: StockReservationService,
        audit_service: AuditService,
        # --- Add Delivery Service ---
        delivery_service: DeliveryService, # <<< Inject DeliveryService
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository # <<< Inject DeliveryRepo
        # ---
    ) -> OrderInDB:
        log = logger.bind(user_id=str(creator.id), channel=order_in.channel)
        log.info("Service: Creating new order...")
        customer_id = creator.id
        customer = await self._validate_customer(customer_id, user_repo)
        # ... (determine profile, process items, generate ref) ...
        try:
            processed_items, total_amount_decimal, stock_updates = await self._process_order_items(...)
        except HTTPException as http_exc:
            # ... (log and re-raise) ...
            raise http_exc
        try:
            order_ref = await counter_service.generate_reference("ORD")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Failed to generate order reference: {e}")

        order_data_internal = OrderCreateInternal(...) # Prepare internal order data

        # --- Reserve Stock ---
        reservation_id = order_ref
        log.info(f"Attempting stock reservation for {len(stock_updates)} items (ResID: {reservation_id})...")
        try:
             await reservation_service.reserve_items_bulk(reservation_id, stock_updates) # Assuming reserve_items_bulk exists
             log.success(f"Stock reservation successful for order {order_ref}.")
        except ReservationError as e:
            log.error(f"Stock reservation failed for order {order_ref}: {e}. Order creation aborted.")
            # No need for manual rollback here if reserve_items_bulk is atomic or handles its own rollback
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT, detail=f"Stock reservation failed: {e}")

        # --- Save Order ---
        created_order_db: Optional[OrderInDB] = None
        try:
            created_order_db = await order_repo.create(order_data_internal.model_dump())
            log.success(f"Order {order_ref} created successfully in DB.")

            # --- >>> Trigger Delivery Creation <<< ---
            try:
                log.info(f"Triggering delivery creation for order {order_ref}...")
                # Pass the created OrderInDB object
                delivery_db = await delivery_service.create_delivery_from_order(
                    order=created_order_db,
                    delivery_repo=delivery_repo,
                    counter_service=counter_service # Delivery needs its own counter
                    # audit_service - handled by delivery service/router? Or pass here?
                )
                # Update order with delivery_id (IMPORTANT)
                await order_repo.update(created_order_db.id, {"delivery_id": delivery_db.id})
                log.info(f"Delivery {delivery_db.delivery_ref} created and linked to order {order_ref}.")
            except Exception as delivery_e:
                # Log error but DON'T fail the order creation because of delivery failure?
                # Or should we try to rollback the order? Depends on business logic.
                # For now, log error and continue returning the created order.
                 log.error(f"Failed to create delivery for order {order_ref} after order creation: {delivery_e}")
            # --- >>> End Delivery Trigger <<< ---

            # await publish_event(...)
            return created_order_db

        except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
            log.exception(f"Failed to save order {order_ref} after reserving stock: {e}")
            log.error("Attempting to release stock reservation as fallback...")
            await reservation_service.release_reservation(reservation_id) # Release general
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Could not save order after reserving stock: {e}")

    # ... (other OrderService methods like update_order_status need modification) ...

    async def update_order_status(
        self,
        order_id_str: str,
        new_status: str,
        notes: Optional[str],
        order_repo: OrderRepository,
        reservation_service: StockReservationService,
        banking_service: BankingService, # Existing
        banking_repo: TransactionRepository, # Existing
        counter_service: CounterService, # Existing for banking
        # stock_service: StockService, # Keep for marking items sold if applicable
        # stock_item_repo: StockItemRepository, # Keep for marking items sold if applicable
        # --- Delivery Related ---
        delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository, # <<< Add Delivery Repo
        # ---
        audit_service: AuditService,
        current_user: Optional[UserInDB] = None # Who is updating?
    ) -> Optional[OrderInDB]:
        log = logger.bind(order_id=order_id_str, new_status=new_status)
        log.info("Service: Updating order status...")
        # ... (fetch order, validate transition) ...
        order_id = order_repo._to_objectid(order_id_str)
        if not order_id: raise HTTPException(400, "Invalid Order ID format")
        order = await order_repo.get_by_id(order_id)
        if not order: return None
        current_status = order.status
        if new_status == current_status: return order
        # ... (Validate transition logic) ...

        # --- Actions based on Transition ---
        reservation_id = order.order_ref
        try:
            # --- Stock Reservation ---
            if new_status in ["cancelled", "failed", "returned"] and current_status != new_status:
                log.debug(f"Releasing stock reservation for order {reservation_id}...")
                await reservation_service.release_reservation(reservation_id)
            elif new_status in ["confirmed", "paid", "processing"] and current_status == "pending":
                log.debug(f"Confirming stock reservation for order {reservation_id}...")
                await reservation_service.confirm_reservation(reservation_id)
        except ReservationError as e:
            log.error(f"Error processing reservation for order {reservation_id}: {e}")
            # Decide how to handle this error (e.g., raise, log, flag order)

        # --- Banking Transaction ---
        # ... (existing logic for sale_income) ...

        # --- >>> Update Delivery Status <<< ---
        # If order is shipped/delivered/returned/cancelled, update corresponding delivery
        delivery_status_map = {
            "shipped": "in_transit",
            "delivered": "delivered",
            "returned": "returned",
            "cancelled": "cancelled",
            "failed": "failed" # Map order failed to delivery failed?
        }
        if new_status in delivery_status_map and order.delivery_id:
            new_delivery_status = delivery_status_map[new_status]
            log.info(f"Updating linked delivery {order.delivery_id} status to '{new_delivery_status}'...")
            try:
                # Use DeliveryService? Or directly update repo? Use repo for simple status change.
                # Need to add tracking event as well. Better use DeliveryService.
                delivery_service : DeliveryService = await get_delivery_service() # Get service instance
                await delivery_service.update_delivery_status(
                    delivery_id_str=str(order.delivery_id),
                    new_status=new_delivery_status,
                    delivery_repo=delivery_repo,
                    notes=f"Order status changed to {new_status}" # Auto note
                    # location - not applicable here?
                    # audit_service - logs handled by delivery service?
                    # current_user - system action?
                )
            except Exception as del_e:
                log.error(f"Failed to update linked delivery {order.delivery_id} status: {del_e}")
        # --- >>> End Delivery Status Update <<< ---

        # --- Final Order Update ---
        log.debug("Updating order document...")
        try:
            update_payload = {"status": new_status}
            if notes is not None: update_payload["notes"] = notes
            # ... (add actual_delivery_date if new_status=='delivered') ...
            updated_db = await order_repo.update(order_id, update_payload)
            if not updated_db:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Failed to finalize order status update.")
            log.success(f"Order {order.order_ref} status updated to {new_status}.")
            # await publish_event(...)
            return updated_db
        except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
            log.error(f"DB error updating final order status {order.order_ref}: {e}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Database error updating order status: {e}")

# ... (get_order_service) ...

python
# app/modules/delivery/routers.py
# ... (imports: APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status, List, Optional, Path, Request) ...
from .services import DeliveryService, get_delivery_service, generate_map_link
from .repository import DeliveryRepository, get_delivery_repository
from .models import (
    DeliveryAPI, TrackingEventAPI, ChatMessageAPI, DeliveryLocationAPI, DeliveryMessageCreateAPI, SENDER_ROLES
)
from app.core.security import CurrentUser, UserInDB, require_role
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository # For enrichment/auth check
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service

delivery_router = APIRouter()

# --- Helper --- (Move to shared dependencies?)
async def get_delivery_or_404(
    delivery_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the Delivery (ObjectId)"),
    delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository = Depends(get_delivery_repository)
) -> DeliveryInDB:
    delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id)
    if not delivery:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="Delivery not found")
    return delivery

# --- Helper Permission Check --- (Refine this)
def check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery: DeliveryInDB, user: UserInDB) -> bool:
    # Who can chat? Customer, Assigned Driver, Admin/Support?
    if not delivery or not user: return False
    is_customer = delivery.customer_id == user.id
    is_driver = delivery.assigned_driver_id and delivery.assigned_driver_id == user.id
    is_staff = any(role in user.roles for role in ["admin", "support", "sales_rep"]) # Define staff roles
    return is_customer or is_driver or is_staff

# --- Endpoints ---

# GET /delivery/{delivery_id}/tracking (Existing or New)
@delivery_router.get(
    "/{delivery_id}/tracking",
    response_model=List[TrackingEventAPI],
    summary="Get delivery tracking history",
    tags=["Delivery"]
    # Add permission checks if needed
)
async def get_delivery_tracking_endpoint(
    delivery: DeliveryInDB = Depends(get_delivery_or_404), # Get delivery or 404
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # For permission check
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = Depends(get_delivery_service)
):
    """Retrieves the list of tracking events for a specific delivery."""
    # Add permission check: e.g., check_delivery_permission(delivery, current_user, action="view_tracking")
    if not check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery, current_user): # Reuse chat permission?
         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized to view tracking")
    return await delivery_service.get_tracking_history(str(delivery.id), delivery_repo=await get_delivery_repository()) # Pass repo

# GET /delivery/{delivery_id}/maplink (NEW)
@delivery_router.get(
    "/{delivery_id}/maplink",
    response_model=DeliveryLocationAPI,
    summary="Get last known location and map link",
    tags=["Delivery"]
    # Add permission checks
)
async def get_delivery_maplink_endpoint(
    delivery: DeliveryInDB = Depends(get_delivery_or_404),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = Depends(get_delivery_service),
):
    """Retrieves the last known location coordinates and a Google Maps link."""
    if not check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery, current_user):
         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized to view location")
    return await delivery_service.get_last_location(str(delivery.id), delivery_repo=await get_delivery_repository())

# GET /delivery/{delivery_id}/chat (NEW)
@delivery_router.get(
    "/{delivery_id}/chat",
    response_model=List[ChatMessageAPI],
    summary="Get delivery chat history",
    tags=["Delivery"]
    # Add permission checks
)
async def get_delivery_chat_endpoint(
    delivery: DeliveryInDB = Depends(get_delivery_or_404),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = Depends(get_delivery_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository), # For enrichment
):
    """Retrieves the chat message history for a specific delivery."""
    if not check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery, current_user):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized to view this chat")
    return await delivery_service.get_chat_history(
        str(delivery.id),
        delivery_repo=await get_delivery_repository(), # Pass repo
        user_repo=user_repo
    )

# POST /delivery/{delivery_id}/message (NEW)
@delivery_router.post(
    "/{delivery_id}/message",
    response_model=ChatMessageAPI, # Return the created message
    status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED,
    summary="Send a message in the delivery chat",
    tags=["Delivery"]
    # Permission checked inside
)
async def send_delivery_message_endpoint(
    payload: DeliveryMessageCreateAPI,
    delivery: DeliveryInDB = Depends(get_delivery_or_404),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = Depends(get_delivery_service),
    delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository = Depends(get_delivery_repository), # Pass to service
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository), # Pass to service
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service), # Pass to service (optional)
):
    """Sends a message associated with a delivery (customer or driver)."""
    # Determine sender role based on user and delivery assignment
    sender_role: Optional[SENDER_ROLES] = None
    if delivery.customer_id == current_user.id:
        sender_role = "customer"
    elif delivery.assigned_driver_id and delivery.assigned_driver_id == current_user.id:
        sender_role = "driver"
    # Allow staff to send messages too?
    elif any(role in current_user.roles for role in ["admin", "support"]):
         sender_role = "driver" # Treat staff sending as if they are the driver/company? Or add 'staff' role? Let's use 'driver' for now.

    if not sender_role:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="User is not authorized to send messages for this delivery.")

    try:
        return await delivery_service.add_chat_message_service(
            delivery_id_str=str(delivery.id),
            message_text=payload.message,
            sender_role=sender_role,
            sender_id=str(current_user.id), # Use the user's actual ID
            delivery_repo=delivery_repo,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service, # Optional
            current_user=current_user # Optional
        )
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc # Repropagate service errors
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Error sending delivery message for {delivery.id}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error sending message.")

python
# app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py
# ... (imports: logger, HTTPException, services, repos, models) ...
from app.modules.delivery.services import DeliveryService, get_delivery_service
from app.modules.delivery.repository import DeliveryRepository, get_delivery_repository
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from app.modules.delivery.models import DeliveryLocationAPI, ChatMessageAPI, SENDER_ROLES # API Models

# --- Action Functions ---

async def send_delivery_message_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> ChatMessageAPI:
    delivery_id = payload.get("delivery_id") # Requires delivery ID or Ref
    message_text = payload.get("message")
    if not delivery_id or not message_text:
        raise ValueError("Missing delivery_id or message for sending message.")

    delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository = await get_delivery_repository()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = await get_delivery_service()

    # Resolve delivery ID (could be Ref from LLM)
    delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id) or await delivery_repo.get_by_ref(delivery_id)
    if not delivery:
        raise ValueError(f"Delivery '{delivery_id}' not found.")

    # Determine sender role (similar logic as in endpoint)
    sender_role: Optional[SENDER_ROLES] = None
    if delivery.customer_id == user.id: sender_role = "customer"
    elif delivery.assigned_driver_id == user.id: sender_role = "driver"
    elif any(role in user.roles for role in ["admin", "support"]): sender_role = "driver" # Staff acts as driver/company

    if not sender_role:
         raise PermissionError("User not authorized to send messages for this delivery.") # Use specific error?

    # Call service (handles validation, saving, WS push)
    # Service returns ChatMessageAPI
    return await delivery_service.add_chat_message_service(
        delivery_id_str=str(delivery.id),
        message_text=message_text,
        sender_role=sender_role,
        sender_id=str(user.id),
        delivery_repo=delivery_repo,
        user_repo=user_repo
        # Audit/CurrentUser handled by dispatcher caller? Or pass None?
    )

async def get_delivery_chat_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> List[ChatMessageAPI]:
    delivery_id = payload.get("delivery_id")
    if not delivery_id: raise ValueError("Missing delivery_id.")

    delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository = await get_delivery_repository()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = await get_delivery_service()

    # Resolve delivery ID
    delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id) or await delivery_repo.get_by_ref(delivery_id)
    if not delivery: raise ValueError(f"Delivery '{delivery_id}' not found.")

    # Permission check
    if not check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery, user): # Reuse check
         raise PermissionError("Not authorized to view this delivery chat.")

    return await delivery_service.get_chat_history(str(delivery.id), delivery_repo, user_repo)


async def get_delivery_location_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> DeliveryLocationAPI:
    delivery_id = payload.get("delivery_id")
    if not delivery_id: raise ValueError("Missing delivery_id.")

    delivery_repo: DeliveryRepository = await get_delivery_repository()
    delivery_service: DeliveryService = await get_delivery_service()

    # Resolve delivery ID
    delivery = await delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id) or await delivery_repo.get_by_ref(delivery_id)
    if not delivery: raise ValueError(f"Delivery '{delivery_id}' not found.")

    # Permission check
    if not check_delivery_chat_permission(delivery, user): # Reuse check
         raise PermissionError("Not authorized to view this delivery location.")

    return await delivery_service.get_last_location(str(delivery.id), delivery_repo)

# --- Update INTENT_ACTION_MAP ---

INTENT_ACTION_MAP: Dict[str, Callable[[Dict[str, Any], UserInDB], Awaitable[Any]]] = {
    # ... (existing intents: create_order, get_my_schedule, etc.) ...
    "send_delivery_message": send_delivery_message_action,
    "get_delivery_chat": get_delivery_chat_action,
    "get_delivery_location": get_delivery_location_action,
    # ...
}

# Ensure main dispatch_intent handles PermissionError appropriately
async def dispatch_intent(intent: str, entities: Dict[str, Any], user: UserInDB) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    # ... (get service_func) ...
    try:
        # ... (validate payload if needed) ...
        result_data = await service_func(payload=validated_payload, user=user)
        return { # Success
            "status": "success",
            "message": f"Action '{intent}' executed.",
            "data": result_data
        }
    except (HTTPException, ValueError) as known_error: # Known errors
        # ... (handle known errors) ...
         error_detail = getattr(known_error, 'detail', str(known_error))
         # ...
         return {"status": "execution_error", "message": error_detail, ...}
    except PermissionError as perm_error: # <<< Handle PermissionError
        log.warning(f"Permission denied during service execution for intent '{intent}': {perm_error}")
        return {
            "status": "permission_denied",
            "message": str(perm_error), # Use message from exception
            "data": None
        }
    except Exception as e: # Unexpected errors
        # ... (handle unexpected errors) ...
        return {"status": "internal_error", ...}

# Add necessary imports like check_delivery_chat_permission, PermissionError, etc.

# app/worker/tasks_delivery.py
from app.worker.celery_app import celery_app
from loguru import logger
from app.core.logging_config import trace_id_var

from datetime import datetime, timedelta, timezone

# Import services/repos needed

@celery_app.task(bind=True, name="delivery.check_location_fallback", max_retries=1)
def check_location_fallback_task(self, delivery_id_str: str, trace_id: Optional[str] = None):

    Celery task to check if delivery location is stale and trigger fallback actions.

    log = logger.bind(trace_id=current_trace_id, task_name=self.name, job_id=self.request.id, delivery_id=delivery_id_str)
    log.info("Running delivery location fallback check...")

    try:
        # --- Implementation Placeholder ---
        log.warning("Delivery location fallback logic not yet implemented.")

        # 4. Fetch Delivery
        # delivery = asyncio.run(delivery_repo.get_by_id(delivery_id))
        # 5. Check status (only run for 'in_transit', 'out_for_delivery'?)

        # 6. Find last tracking event WITH location
        # last_loc_event = next((e for e in delivery.tracking_history if e.location), None)
        # last_loc_time = last_loc_event.timestamp if last_loc_event else delivery.created_at # Fallback?
        # 7. Compare with threshold
        # if datetime.now(timezone.utc) - last_loc_time > timedelta(minutes=threshold_minutes):

        log.exception("Error during delivery location fallback check.")

        # self.retry(exc=e, countdown=60)
        return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
    finally:
        trace_id_var.reset(token)

item_3_prompt = """

### MISSÃO: Implementar o Item 3 do Roadmap Urgente

**Título:** Autoescala de turnos baseada em saldo e perfil (scheduling)

---

### FUNCIONALIDADES:

1. **Criação de turnos por unidade/data/perfil**
   - Schema: `ShiftCreateAPI` com campos como `unit_id`, `start_time`, `end_time`, `required_role`, `max_participants`
   - Modelo interno: `ShiftInDB` com lista `assigned_users: List[UserAssignment]`

2. **Autoatribuição de usuários com saldo disponível**
   - Serviço: `SchedulingService.auto_assign_users(shift: ShiftInDB)`
     - Filtra usuários ativos com saldo suficiente e papel compatível
     - Seleciona até `max_participants` usando critério FIFO ou score
     - Atualiza `assigned_users`, debita saldo (via BankingService)

3. **Endpoints necessários**
   - `POST /shifts/auto-assign` – cria e preenche turno automaticamente
   - `GET /shifts/{id}` – retorna dados do turno com usuários atribuídos
   - `GET /users/{id}/schedule` – retorna próximos turnos do usuário

4. **Intents no dispatcher**
   - `create_auto_shift`: cria turno ideal para hoje baseado no perfil
   - `get_my_schedule`: retorna turnos atribuídos ao usuário atual

5. **Validações**
   - Não agendar usuário já escalado no mesmo período
   - Checar saldo antes de atribuir
   - Permitir score ou prioridade (ex: usuários preferenciais)

---

### COMO ENTREGAR

Para cada funcionalidade:
- Gere os schemas (input/output)
- Crie a lógica do serviço de autoescala
- Adicione as rotas REST
- Mapeie os intents no dispatcher
- Siga padrões do AgentOS

Nada de explicações. Apenas entrega.
"""

python
# app/modules/scheduling/models.py
# ... (imports: BaseModel, Field, Literal, datetime, date, time, ObjectId, Decimal, PyObjectId, ConfigDict, field_validator) ...
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any

SHIFT_STATUSES = Literal["pending_assignment", "assigned", "in_progress", "completed", "cancelled"] # New status flow
ASSIGNMENT_STATUS = Literal["pending", "confirmed", "rejected"]

# --- Sub-Schemas ---
class UserAssignment(BaseModel):
    user_id: ObjectId
    # status: ASSIGNMENT_STATUS = "pending" # Maybe track confirmation? Keep simple first.
    assigned_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    # Add score/priority if used for selection?

# --- Internal/DB Models ---

# Modify ShiftBase and add new fields
class ShiftBase(BaseModel):
    # unit_id: Optional[str] = Field(None, description="Identifier for the work unit/location") # Optional unit/location
    shift_date: date = Field(...)
    start_time: time = Field(...)
    end_time: time = Field(...)
    required_role: Optional[str] = Field(None, description="Role required for this shift") # Role requirement
    max_participants: int = Field(default=1, gt=0, description="Maximum number of users for this shift") # Max users
    required_balance: Decimal = Field(default=Decimal("0.00"), description="Minimum balance required to be assigned") # Balance requirement

    # Validator to ensure end_time is after start_time
    @field_validator('end_time')
    @classmethod
    def check_end_time(cls, v: time, info):
        if 'start_time' in info.data and v <= info.data['start_time']:
            raise ValueError('End time must be after start time')
        return v

# Modify ShiftCreateInternal
class ShiftCreateInternal(ShiftBase):
    status: SHIFT_STATUSES = "pending_assignment" # Default status before auto-assign
    notes: Optional[str] = None
    assigned_users: List[UserAssignment] = Field(default_factory=list) # Initialize empty

# Modify ShiftUpdateInternal
class ShiftUpdateInternal(BaseModel):
    status: Optional[SHIFT_STATUSES] = None
    notes: Optional[str] = None
    # Add other updatable fields if needed

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra='ignore')

# Modify ShiftInDB
class ShiftInDB(ShiftBase):
    id: PyObjectId = Field(..., alias="_id")
    status: SHIFT_STATUSES
    notes: Optional[str] = None
    assigned_users: List[UserAssignment] = Field(default_factory=list) # List of assigned user info
    # Remove payment fields? Payment is handled elsewhere based on attendance/completion? Yes.
    # paid_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    # paid_amount: Optional[str] = None
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

    model_config = ConfigDict(
        populate_by_name=True,
        arbitrary_types_allowed=True,
        json_encoders={ObjectId: str, datetime: lambda dt: dt.isoformat(), date: lambda d: d.isoformat(), time: lambda t: t.isoformat(), Decimal: str}
    )

# --- API Models ---

# Modify ShiftAPI to show assigned users (maybe just count or names?)
class AssignedUserAPI(BaseModel):
    user_id: str
    user_name: Optional[str] = None # Enriched

class ShiftAPI(BaseModel):
    id: str
    shift_date: date
    start_time: time
    end_time: time
    required_role: Optional[str] = None
    max_participants: int
    required_balance: str # Return Decimal as string
    status: SHIFT_STATUSES
    # location: Optional[str] = None # If using unit_id
    notes: Optional[str] = None
    assigned_users: List[AssignedUserAPI] = Field(default_factory=list) # Enriched list
    assigned_count: int = 0 # Convenience field
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime

    model_config = ConfigDict(
        from_attributes=True,
        json_encoders={datetime: lambda dt: dt.isoformat() if dt else None, date: lambda d: d.isoformat(), time: lambda t: t.isoformat()}
    )

# API Model for creating a shift and triggering auto-assignment
class AutoAssignShiftCreateAPI(BaseModel):
    # unit_id: Optional[str] = None
    shift_date: date
    start_time: time
    end_time: time
    required_role: Optional[str] = None
    max_participants: int = Field(default=1, gt=0)
    required_balance: str = Field(default="0.00", description="Min balance as string") # Receive as string
    notes: Optional[str] = None
    # Optional: Add selection criteria (fifo, score_based) ? Keep simple first.

    _required_balance_decimal: Optional[Decimal] = None # Private field for validated decimal

    @field_validator('required_balance')
    @classmethod
    def validate_balance_str(cls, v: str) -> str:
        try:
            # Validate and store decimal internally for service use
            cls._required_balance_decimal = Decimal(v).quantize(Decimal("0.01"))
            if cls._required_balance_decimal < Decimal("0.00"):
                 raise ValueError("Required balance cannot be negative")
            return v # Keep string in the model
        except InvalidOperation:
            raise ValueError("Invalid format for required_balance. Use string like '10.00'.")

    @field_validator('end_time')
    @classmethod
    def check_end_time(cls, v: time, info):
        if 'start_time' in info.data and v <= info.data['start_time']:
            raise ValueError('End time must be after start time')
        return v

# API Model for response of auto-assignment
class AutoAssignResponseAPI(BaseModel):
    message: str
    shift: ShiftAPI # Return the created/assigned shift
    assigned_count: int
    unfilled_slots: int

**2. Lógica (Service & Repository)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/scheduling/repository.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/scheduling/repository.py
# ... (imports: ObjectId, logger, etc) ...
from .models import ShiftInDB, ShiftCreateInternal, ShiftUpdateInternal, UserAssignment

class ShiftRepository(BaseRepository[ShiftInDB, ShiftCreateInternal, ShiftUpdateInternal]):
    # ... (existing create_indexes, _prepare_data_for_db) ...

    # Modify list_shifts_by_user_and_date to query assigned_users array
    async def list_shifts_by_user_and_date(
        self,
        user_id: ObjectId,
        start_date: date,
        end_date: date,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 31
    ) -> List[ShiftInDB]:
        """Lists shifts where the user is assigned within a date range."""
        query = {
            "assigned_users.user_id": user_id, # Query the array
            "shift_date": {"$gte": start_date, "$lte": end_date}
        }
        sort_order = [("shift_date", ASCENDING), ("start_time", ASCENDING)]
        return await self.list_by(query=query, skip=skip, limit=limit, sort=sort_order)

    async def check_user_already_assigned(
        self,
        user_id: ObjectId,
        shift_date: date,
        start_time: time,
        end_time: time
    ) -> bool:
        """Checks if a user is already assigned to ANY shift overlapping the given time."""
        # Define the time window for the potential new shift
        # Combine date and time for comparison (store date only, compare ranges)
        # A simpler check: is user assigned to ANY shift on that specific date?
        query = {
            "assigned_users.user_id": user_id,
            "shift_date": shift_date,
            # Add stricter time overlap check if needed (more complex query)
        }
        count = await self.collection.count_documents(query)
        return count > 0

    async def add_assigned_users_to_shift(
        self,
        shift_id: ObjectId,
        assignments: List[UserAssignment]
    ) -> bool:
        """Adds users to the assigned_users list and updates status."""
        if not assignments:
            return False
        log = logger.bind(shift_id=str(shift_id), assign_count=len(assignments))
        log.info("Adding assigned users to shift...")
        user_assignment_dicts = [a.model_dump(mode='json') for a in assignments]
        try:
            result: UpdateResult = await self.collection.update_one(
                {"_id": shift_id},
                {
                    "$push": {"assigned_users": {"$each": user_assignment_dicts}},
                    "$set": {"status": "assigned", "updated_at": datetime.utcnow()} # Update status
                }
            )
            success = result.modified_count > 0
            if success: log.success("Users added to shift assignment.")
            else: log.warning("Failed to add users to shift (not found or no changes?).")
            return success
        except Exception as e:
            self._handle_db_exception(e, "add_assigned_users_to_shift", shift_id)
            return False

# ... (get_shift_repository) ...

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/scheduling/services.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/scheduling/services.py
# ... (imports: Optional, List, Dict, Any, datetime, date, time, ObjectId, HTTPException, status, logger, Decimal) ...
from .repository import ShiftRepository
from .models import ShiftInDB, ShiftCreateInternal, UserAssignment, ShiftAPI, AssignedUserAPI
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository
from app.modules.people.models import UserInDB
from app.modules.banking.services import BankingService, get_banking_service # For balance deduction
from app.modules.banking.repository import TransactionRepository, get_transaction_repository # For balance deduction
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService # Optional
from app.core.counters import CounterService # Needed by BankingService

class SchedulingService:
    # ... (existing _enrich_shift - modify to handle assigned_users, create_shift, list_shifts_for_user, get_shift) ...

    async def _enrich_shift(self, shift_db: ShiftInDB, user_repo: UserRepository) -> ShiftAPI:
        """Enriches shift with assigned user details."""
        # Base validation/conversion
        shift_api = ShiftAPI(
            id=str(shift_db.id),
            shift_date=shift_db.shift_date,
            start_time=shift_db.start_time,
            end_time=shift_db.end_time,
            required_role=shift_db.required_role,
            max_participants=shift_db.max_participants,
            required_balance=str(shift_db.required_balance), # Format Decimal to string
            status=shift_db.status,
            notes=shift_db.notes,
            assigned_users=[], # Initialize empty
            assigned_count=len(shift_db.assigned_users),
            created_at=shift_db.created_at,
            updated_at=shift_db.updated_at,
        )

        # Enrich assigned users
        assigned_user_ids = [ua.user_id for ua in shift_db.assigned_users]
        if assigned_user_ids:
            users = await user_repo.list_by({"_id": {"$in": assigned_user_ids}}, limit=0) # Fetch all assigned
            user_map = {str(u.id): u for u in users}
            enriched_assignments = []
            for ua in shift_db.assigned_users:
                user = user_map.get(str(ua.user_id))
                enriched_assignments.append(AssignedUserAPI(
                    user_id=str(ua.user_id),
                    user_name=f"{user.profile.first_name or ''} {user.profile.last_name or ''}".strip() if user and user.profile else "Unknown User"
                ))
            shift_api.assigned_users = enriched_assignments

        return shift_api

    # Modify list_shifts_for_user to use repo method
    async def list_shifts_for_user(
        self,
        user_id: ObjectId,
        start_date: date,
        end_date: date,
        shift_repo: ShiftRepository,
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 31
    ) -> List[ShiftAPI]:
        log = logger.bind(service="SchedulingService", user_id=str(user_id), start=start_date, end=end_date)
        log.debug("Service: Listing shifts assigned to user...")
        # Use the repository method that queries assigned_users
        shifts_db = await shift_repo.list_shifts_by_user_and_date(user_id, start_date, end_date, skip, limit)
        enriched_shifts = [await self._enrich_shift(s, user_repo) for s in shifts_db]
        log.info(f"Found {len(enriched_shifts)} assigned shifts for user.")
        return enriched_shifts

    # --- Auto-Assignment Logic ---
    async def auto_assign_users_to_shift(
        self,
        shift: ShiftInDB, # The newly created shift object (status='pending_assignment')
        shift_repo: ShiftRepository,
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        banking_service: BankingService,
        banking_repo: TransactionRepository, # Needed by banking service
        counter_service: CounterService, # Needed by banking service
        audit_service: Optional[AuditService] = None,
        actor: Optional[UserInDB] = None # Admin/System performing the action
    ) -> Tuple[int, List[ObjectId]]: # Returns (assigned_count, list_of_assigned_user_ids)
        """
        Finds eligible users and assigns them to the shift, deducting balance.
        """
        log = logger.bind(service="SchedulingService", shift_id=str(shift.id), date=shift.shift_date)
        log.info(f"Starting auto-assignment: Max={shift.max_participants}, Role={shift.required_role}, Balance>={shift.required_balance}")

        if shift.status != "pending_assignment":
            log.warning(f"Shift is not pending assignment (status: {shift.status}). Skipping auto-assign.")
            return 0, []

        slots_to_fill = shift.max_participants
        assignments: List[UserAssignment] = []
        assigned_user_ids: List[ObjectId] = []

        # 1. Find Eligible Users
        query: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "is_active": True,
            "profile.balance": {"$gte": str(shift.required_balance)} # Compare balance string
        }
        if shift.required_role:
            query["roles"] = shift.required_role

        # TODO: Implement scoring/prioritization here if needed. Default: FIFO (use created_at sort?)
        sort_criteria = [("created_at", ASCENDING)] # Simple FIFO based on user creation date
        eligible_users_cursor = user_repo.collection.find(query).sort(sort_criteria)

        # 2. Iterate and Assign (checking schedule conflicts)
        async for user_doc in eligible_users_cursor:
            if len(assignments) >= slots_to_fill:
                break # Filled all slots

            user = UserInDB.model_validate(user_doc) # Validate data
            user_id = user.id
            log.debug(f"Checking eligibility for user {user.email} (ID: {user_id})")

            # Check if already assigned to an overlapping shift (basic date check for now)
            is_already_assigned = await shift_repo.check_user_already_assigned(
                user_id, shift.shift_date, shift.start_time, shift.end_time
            )
            if is_already_assigned:
                log.debug(f"User {user.email} already assigned on {shift.shift_date}. Skipping.")
                continue

            # 3. Balance Deduction (Simulated - requires BankingService integration)
            try:
                log.info(f"Attempting balance deduction for user {user.email}...")
                # Use BankingService to create a transaction (e.g., 'shift_assignment_fee')
                # The BankingService's record_transaction should handle the balance update via UserService
                deduction_amount = shift.required_balance # Or a fixed fee? Use required_balance for now
                if deduction_amount > Decimal("0.00"): # Only deduct if required balance > 0
                    transaction_internal = TransactionCreateInternal(
                         type="expense_shift_fee", # Define a new transaction type
                         amount=-deduction_amount, # Negative for deduction
                         currency="BRL", # Or from settings
                         description=f"Fee/Hold for shift {shift.id} on {shift.shift_date}",
                         status="completed", # Assume deduction is immediate
                         associated_user_id=user_id,
                         # associated_order_id = shift.id? Link to shift? Add field to Transaction model?
                     )
                    # Get dependencies for banking service call
                    await banking_service.record_transaction(
                         transaction_in=transaction_internal,
                         banking_repo=banking_repo,
                         counter_service=counter_service,
                         audit_service=audit_service,
                         user_service=await get_user_service(), # Get dependencies within async context
                         user_repo=user_repo,
                         current_user=actor # Log who triggered the deduction (system/admin)
                    )
                    log.success(f"Balance deduction successful for user {user.email}.")
                else:
                     log.info("No balance deduction required for this shift.")

                # If deduction successful (or not needed), add to assignment list
                assignments.append(UserAssignment(user_id=user_id))
                assigned_user_ids.append(user_id)

            except Exception as e:
                # If balance deduction fails, DO NOT assign the user
                log.error(f"Balance deduction FAILED for user {user.email}: {e}. Skipping assignment.")
                # TODO: Should we attempt to rollback the transaction if partially created? Complex.
                continue # Skip this user

        # 4. Update Shift with Assignments
        if assignments:
            success = await shift_repo.add_assigned_users_to_shift(shift.id, assignments)
            if success:
                log.info(f"Successfully assigned {len(assignments)} users to shift {shift.id}.")
            else:
                log.error(f"Failed to update shift {shift.id} with assignments in DB after processing users.")
                # Critical error: Users might have had balance deducted but aren't assigned.
                # Need manual intervention or more robust rollback.
                # For now, just log the error.
        elif slots_to_fill > 0:
            log.warning(f"Could not find enough eligible users to fill shift {shift.id}. Assigned: 0")
            # Keep status as 'pending_assignment'? Or move to 'unfilled'? Let's keep pending.
            pass

        assigned_count = len(assignments)
        return assigned_count, assigned_user_ids

# ... (get_scheduling_service) ...

# Add necessary imports at the top
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation
from app.modules.banking.models import TransactionCreateInternal # For balance deduction
from app.modules.people.services import get_user_service # For balance deduction
from pymongo import ASCENDING # For sorting

**3. Endpoints (Rotas)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/scheduling/routers.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/scheduling/routers.py
# ... (imports: APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status, List, Optional, Path, Request, date, time) ...
from .services import SchedulingService, get_scheduling_service
from .repository import ShiftRepository, get_shift_repository
from .models import ShiftAPI, AutoAssignShiftCreateAPI, AutoAssignResponseAPI, ShiftInDB # Import new API models
from app.core.security import CurrentUser, UserInDB, require_role
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from app.modules.banking.services import BankingService, get_banking_service # For auto-assign
from app.modules.banking.repository import TransactionRepository, get_transaction_repository # For auto-assign
from app.core.counters import CounterService, get_counter_service # For auto-assign banking call
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service

scheduling_router = APIRouter()

# --- Admin Endpoint for Auto-Assign ---
@scheduling_router.post(
    "/auto-assign",
    response_model=AutoAssignResponseAPI, # Custom response
    status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "manager"]))],
    summary="Create shift and auto-assign users (Admin)",
    tags=["Scheduling - Admin"]
)
async def create_and_auto_assign_shift(
    request: Request,
    shift_create_payload: AutoAssignShiftCreateAPI, # New API model for input
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    scheduling_service: SchedulingService = Depends(get_scheduling_service),
    shift_repo: ShiftRepository = Depends(get_shift_repository),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository),
    banking_service: BankingService = Depends(get_banking_service), # <<< Inject Banking Service
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = Depends(get_transaction_repository), # <<< Inject Banking Repo
    counter_service: CounterService = Depends(get_counter_service), # <<< Inject Counter Service
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service)
):
    """
    (Admin/Manager Only) Creates a new shift based on requirements and automatically
    assigns eligible users based on role, balance, and availability.
    """
    log = logger.bind(user_id=str(current_user.id))
    log.info(f"Endpoint: Creating and auto-assigning shift for date {shift_create_payload.shift_date}...")

    # 1. Prepare internal shift creation data
    try:
        # Use the validated Decimal from the Pydantic model
        required_balance_dec = shift_create_payload._required_balance_decimal or Decimal("0.00")

        shift_internal_create = ShiftCreateInternal(
            shift_date=shift_create_payload.shift_date,
            start_time=shift_create_payload.start_time,
            end_time=shift_create_payload.end_time,
            required_role=shift_create_payload.required_role,
            max_participants=shift_create_payload.max_participants,
            required_balance=required_balance_dec,
            notes=shift_create_payload.notes,
            status="pending_assignment" # Start in pending state
        )
    except Exception as pydantic_err: # Catch validation errors if any slipped through
         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Invalid shift data: {pydantic_err}")

    # 2. Create the Shift document first
    try:
        # Use repo directly to create the shift structure initially
        # Service create might have extra logic not needed here yet
        created_shift_db = await shift_repo.create(shift_internal_create.model_dump())
        log.info(f"Shift structure created (ID: {created_shift_db.id}), proceeding to auto-assignment.")
    except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
        log.error(f"Failed to create initial shift document: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Could not create shift structure: {e}")

    # 3. Call the auto-assignment service logic
    try:
        assigned_count, _ = await scheduling_service.auto_assign_users_to_shift(
            shift=created_shift_db, # Pass the created DB object
            shift_repo=shift_repo,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            banking_service=banking_service,
            banking_repo=banking_repo,
            counter_service=counter_service,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            actor=current_user
        )
    except Exception as assign_e:
        # If assignment fails critically AFTER shift creation, what to do?
        # Keep the shift as pending? Delete it? Mark as failed_assignment?
        # For now, log error and return the shift as pending.
        log.exception(f"Error during auto-assignment for shift {created_shift_db.id}: {assign_e}")
        # Optionally update shift status to an error state here
        # await shift_repo.update(created_shift_db.id, {"status": "failed_assignment", "notes": f"Auto-assign error: {assign_e}"})
        # Reraise or return gracefully? Return gracefully for now.
        final_shift_db = await shift_repo.get_by_id(created_shift_db.id) # Get potentially updated state
        final_shift_api = await scheduling_service._enrich_shift(final_shift_db, user_repo)
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Shift created but auto-assignment failed: {assign_e}")

    # 4. Fetch final shift state and prepare response
    final_shift_db = await shift_repo.get_by_id(created_shift_db.id)
    if not final_shift_db: # Should not happen
         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Failed to retrieve shift after assignment.")

    final_shift_api = await scheduling_service._enrich_shift(final_shift_db, user_repo)
    unfilled_slots = max(0, final_shift_api.max_participants - assigned_count)
    message = f"Shift created. Auto-assigned {assigned_count} user(s)."
    if unfilled_slots > 0:
        message += f" ({unfilled_slots} slots remain unfilled)."

    await audit_service.log_audit_event(
         action="shift_auto_assigned", status="success", entity_type="Shift",
         entity_id=final_shift_api.id, audit_repo=None,
         details={"assigned": assigned_count, "max": final_shift_api.max_participants, "role": final_shift_api.required_role},
         current_user=current_user, request=request
     )

    return AutoAssignResponseAPI(
        message=message,
        shift=final_shift_api,
        assigned_count=assigned_count,
        unfilled_slots=unfilled_slots
    )


# Modify GET /shifts/{id} (Admin/User) - Need to check permissions carefully
@scheduling_router.get(
    "/{shift_id}",
    response_model=ShiftAPI,
    summary="Get specific shift details",
    tags=["Scheduling", "Scheduling - Admin"] # Add to both?
)
async def get_shift_details(
    shift: ShiftInDB = Depends(get_shift_or_404),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    scheduling_service: SchedulingService = Depends(get_scheduling_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository)
):
    """Retrieves details for a specific shift."""
    # Permission check: Allow admin/manager OR an assigned user to view
    is_admin_manager = any(role in current_user.roles for role in ["admin", "manager"])
    is_assigned = any(ua.user_id == current_user.id for ua in shift.assigned_users)

    if not is_admin_manager and not is_assigned:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized to view this shift.")

    return await scheduling_service._enrich_shift(shift, user_repo)


# Modify GET /me to use the correct service method
@scheduling_router.get(
    "/me",
    response_model=List[ShiftAPI],
    summary="Get my assigned schedule", # Changed description
    tags=["Scheduling"]
)
async def get_my_assigned_schedule( # Renamed function
    start_date: date = Query(..., description="Start date (YYYY-MM-DD)"),
    end_date: date = Query(..., description="End date (YYYY-MM-DD)"),
    skip: int = Query(0, ge=0),
    limit: int = Query(31, ge=1, le=100),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    scheduling_service: SchedulingService = Depends(get_scheduling_service),
    shift_repo: ShiftRepository = Depends(get_shift_repository), # Pass repo
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository) # Pass repo
):
    """Retrieves the shifts the currently logged-in user is assigned to."""
    if start_date > end_date: raise HTTPException(400, "Start date cannot be after end date")
    # Use the updated service method
    return await scheduling_service.list_shifts_for_user(
        user_id=current_user.id, start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date,
        shift_repo=shift_repo, user_repo=user_repo, skip=skip, limit=limit
    )

python
# app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py
# ... (imports: logger, HTTPException, services, repos, models, date, timedelta, Decimal, etc) ...
from app.modules.scheduling.services import SchedulingService, get_scheduling_service
from app.modules.scheduling.repository import ShiftRepository, get_shift_repository
from app.modules.scheduling.models import ShiftAPI, AutoAssignShiftCreateAPI, AutoAssignResponseAPI # API Models
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from app.modules.banking.services import BankingService, get_banking_service
from app.modules.banking.repository import TransactionRepository, get_transaction_repository
from app.core.counters import CounterService, get_counter_service
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service


# --- Action Functions ---

async def create_auto_shift_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> AutoAssignResponseAPI:
    """
    Action function for 'create_auto_shift' intent.
    Parses LLM payload and calls the POST /shifts/auto-assign logic (simulated).
    Requires admin/manager privileges implicitly checked by endpoint/service.
    """
    log = logger.bind(intent="create_auto_shift", user_id=str(user.id))
    log.info("Executing create_auto_shift action...")

    # Assume LLM provides necessary details in payload
    try:
        # Validate/parse payload from LLM entities into the API model format
        # This requires robust entity extraction from the LLM prompt
        shift_create_api_payload = AutoAssignShiftCreateAPI.model_validate(payload)
        # Example: payload = {"shift_date": "2024-12-25", "start_time": "09:00", "end_time": "17:00", "max_participants": 2, "required_role": "cashier", "required_balance": "5.00"}

    except ValidationError as e:
        log.warning(f"Validation failed for create_auto_shift payload: {e.errors()}")
        raise ValueError(f"Missing or invalid information for shift creation: {e.errors()}")

    # Get dependencies (could be cached or fetched fresh)
    scheduling_service: SchedulingService = await get_scheduling_service()
    shift_repo: ShiftRepository = await get_shift_repository()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()
    banking_service: BankingService = await get_banking_service()
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = await get_transaction_repository()
    counter_service: CounterService = await get_counter_service()
    audit_service: AuditService = await get_audit_service()

    # Simulate calling the logic similar to the /auto-assign endpoint
    # Create Shift Structure
    try:
        required_balance_dec = shift_create_api_payload._required_balance_decimal or Decimal("0.00")
        shift_internal_create = ShiftCreateInternal(
            shift_date=shift_create_api_payload.shift_date,
            start_time=shift_create_api_payload.start_time,
            end_time=shift_create_api_payload.end_time,
            required_role=shift_create_api_payload.required_role,
            max_participants=shift_create_api_payload.max_participants,
            required_balance=required_balance_dec,
            notes=shift_create_api_payload.notes,
            status="pending_assignment"
        )
        created_shift_db = await shift_repo.create(shift_internal_create.model_dump())
    except Exception as e:
         log.error(f"Failed creating initial shift document via dispatcher: {e}")
         raise RuntimeError(f"Could not create shift structure: {e}") # Let main handler catch

    # Auto-Assign
    try:
         assigned_count, _ = await scheduling_service.auto_assign_users_to_shift(
             shift=created_shift_db,
             shift_repo=shift_repo, user_repo=user_repo,
             banking_service=banking_service, banking_repo=banking_repo,
             counter_service=counter_service, audit_service=audit_service,
             actor=user # User initiating via LLM is the actor
         )
    except Exception as e:
         log.exception(f"Error during auto-assignment via dispatcher for shift {created_shift_db.id}: {e}")
         # Return partial success? Or error? Error is safer.
         raise RuntimeError(f"Shift created but auto-assignment failed: {e}")

    # Fetch final state and return structured response
    final_shift_db = await shift_repo.get_by_id(created_shift_db.id)
    final_shift_api = await scheduling_service._enrich_shift(final_shift_db, user_repo)
    unfilled = max(0, final_shift_api.max_participants - assigned_count)
    msg = f"Shift created for {final_shift_api.shift_date}. Auto-assigned {assigned_count} user(s)."
    if unfilled > 0: msg += f" ({unfilled} slots remain)."

    response = AutoAssignResponseAPI(
        message=msg, shift=final_shift_api, assigned_count=assigned_count, unfilled_slots=unfilled
    )
    # Return as dict for dispatcher
    return response.model_dump(mode='json')

# Reuse get_my_schedule_action from previous step for 'get_my_schedule' intent
