python
# app/modules/people/models.py
# ... (imports: BaseModel, Field, EmailStr, ConfigDict, List, Optional, Dict, Any, datetime, ObjectId, Decimal, PyObjectId) ...

# --- Constants ---
USER_ROLES = Literal["admin", "driver", "customer", "reseller", "support", "manager", "system"] # Expanded roles

# --- Internal/DB Models ---

# Modify UserProfile to be more complete
class UserProfile(BaseModel):
    first_name: Optional[str] = None
    last_name: Optional[str] = None
    phone: Optional[str] = None
    document: Optional[str] = Field(None, description="CPF/CNPJ or other document") # <<< ADDED document
    address: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = Field(None, description="Standard address object") # <<< ADDED address
    photo_url: Optional[str] = Field(None, description="URL for user's profile picture") # <<< ADDED photo_url
    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list, description="General purpose tags") # <<< ADDED tags
    balance: Decimal = Field(default=Decimal("0.00"), description="Customer balance. Negative means debt.") # Existing

    model_config = ConfigDict(arbitrary_types_allowed=True)

# Modify UserCreateInternal if needed (e.g., allow setting roles/profile on creation)
class UserCreateInternal(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    hashed_password: str
    profile: UserProfile = Field(default_factory=UserProfile)
    roles: List[USER_ROLES] = ["customer"] # Use Literal for roles
    is_active: bool = True
    # rfid_tags: Optional[List[str]] = None # Keep if using RFID

# Modify UserUpdateInternal for profile fields, roles, balance
class UserUpdateInternal(BaseModel):
    email: Optional[EmailStr] = None
    hashed_password: Optional[str] = None # Should have separate password change endpoint
    profile: Optional[UserProfile] = None # Allow updating profile object
    roles: Optional[List[USER_ROLES]] = None # <<< Allow role update (admin only?)
    is_active: Optional[bool] = None
    # rfid_tags: Optional[List[str]] = None
    # balance: Optional[Decimal] = None # Balance adjustment should be explicit action, not direct set

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra='ignore')

# Modify UserInDB to reflect profile changes and roles
class UserInDB(BaseModel):
    id: PyObjectId = Field(default_factory=PyObjectId, alias="_id")
    email: EmailStr
    hashed_password: str
    profile: UserProfile = Field(default_factory=UserProfile)
    roles: List[USER_ROLES] = Field(default=["customer"]) # Use Literal
    is_active: bool = Field(default=True)
    # rfid_tags: Optional[List[str]] = None
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

    # Balance is implicitly in profile now, no need to duplicate here
    # balance: Decimal = Field(default=Decimal("0.00"))

    model_config = ConfigDict(
        populate_by_name=True,
        arbitrary_types_allowed=True,
        json_encoders={ObjectId: str, datetime: lambda dt: dt.isoformat(), Decimal: str}
    )


# --- API Models ---

# API Model for Profile (subset of internal, maybe exclude balance?)
class UserProfileAPI(BaseModel):
    first_name: Optional[str] = None
    last_name: Optional[str] = None
    phone: Optional[str] = None
    document: Optional[str] = None
    address: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    photo_url: Optional[str] = None
    tags: List[str] = []
    # Exclude balance from public profile API? Yes. Balance via specific endpoint.

# API Model for User Output (used for /me and listing users)
class UserAPI(BaseModel):
    id: str # Return ID as string
    email: EmailStr
    profile: UserProfileAPI # Use the API profile model
    roles: List[USER_ROLES] # Use Literal
    is_active: bool
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime
    # rfid_tags: Optional[List[str]] = None

    model_config = ConfigDict(from_attributes=True)

# API Model for Creating Users (Admin)
class UserCreateAdminAPI(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    password: str = Field(..., min_length=8)
    profile: Optional[UserProfileAPI] = None # Profile optional on creation
    roles: List[USER_ROLES] = ["customer"] # Default roles
    is_active: bool = True

# API Model for Updating User Profile (by self or admin)
class UserProfileUpdateAPI(BaseModel):
    first_name: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=1)
    last_name: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=1)
    phone: Optional[str] = None
    document: Optional[str] = None
    address: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    photo_url: Optional[str] = None
    tags: Optional[List[str]] = None
    # Balance NOT updatable via profile patch

# API Model for Admin Updating User (Roles, Status)
class UserAdminUpdateAPI(BaseModel):
    roles: Optional[List[USER_ROLES]] = None
    is_active: Optional[bool] = None

# API Model for Balance Adjustment Payload
class AdjustBalancePayloadAPI(BaseModel):
    amount: str = Field(..., description="Amount to adjust as string (e.g., '10.50' or '-5.00')")
    reason: str = Field(..., min_length=5, description="Mandatory reason for the adjustment")
    order_ref: Optional[str] = Field(None, description="Optional linked order reference")

    _amount_decimal: Optional[Decimal] = None # For validation

    @field_validator('amount')
    @classmethod
    def validate_amount_str(cls, v: str) -> str:
        try:
            cls._amount_decimal = Decimal(v).quantize(Decimal("0.01"))
            # Allow zero adjustment? Maybe for correction notes? Allow for now.
            # if cls._amount_decimal == Decimal("0.00"): raise ValueError("Adjustment amount cannot be zero")
            return v
        except InvalidOperation:
            raise ValueError("Invalid amount format. Use string like '10.50'.")

**2. Lógica (Service & Repository)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/people/repository.py (No changes needed beyond previous balance update)**
*(The update_balance method added previously is sufficient for adjustments.)*

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/people/services.py (Modify/Add)**

python
# app/modules/people/services.py
# ... (imports: UserInDB, UserRepository, UserProfile, UserCreateInternal, UserUpdateInternal, ...)
from .models import UserAPI, UserProfileAPI, UserProfileUpdateAPI, USER_ROLES # API Models
from app.core.security import get_password_hash, verify_password # Security utils
from app.modules.banking.services import BankingService # Needed if adjustment creates transaction

class UserService:
    # ... (authenticate - should be fine) ...

    async def create_user( # Modified for admin creation potentially
        self,
        user_data: UserCreateInternal, # Accepts internal model
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        audit_service: Optional[AuditService] = None,
        creator: Optional[UserInDB] = None # Who is creating?
    ) -> UserInDB: # Returns DB model
        log = logger.bind(service="UserService", email=user_data.email)
        log.info("Service: Creating new user...")
        # Hash password before sending to repo
        # Password hashing should happen here, not in repo
        user_data.hashed_password = get_password_hash(user_data.hashed_password) # Assume password is plain here

        try:
            created_db = await user_repo.create(user_data) # Repo handles lowercase email
            log.success(f"User created successfully. ID: {created_db.id}")
            if audit_service:
                await audit_service.log_audit_event(
                    action="user_created", status="success", entity_type="User",
                    entity_id=created_db.id, audit_repo=None,
                    details={"email": created_db.email, "roles": created_db.roles},
                    current_user=creator, request=None
                )
            return created_db
        except ValueError as ve: # Duplicate email from repo
            log.warning(f"User creation failed: {ve}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT, detail=str(ve))
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception("Unexpected error creating user.")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, detail="Could not create user.")

    async def get_user_by_id(self, user_id_str: str, user_repo: UserRepository) -> Optional[UserInDB]:
        # Simple fetch, repo handles ID conversion
        return await user_repo.get_by_id(user_id_str)

    async def get_user_profile_api(self, user_db: UserInDB) -> UserProfileAPI:
        """Converts UserInDB profile to UserProfileAPI (excluding balance)."""
        return UserProfileAPI.model_validate(user_db.profile.model_dump(exclude={'balance'}))

    async def update_user_profile(
        self,
        user_to_update: UserInDB, # The user object being updated
        profile_update_data: UserProfileUpdateAPI, # API model for update payload
        updater: UserInDB, # The user performing the update
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        audit_service: AuditService
    ) -> UserInDB:
        log = logger.bind(service="UserService", target_user_id=str(user_to_update.id), updater_id=str(updater.id))
        log.info("Service: Updating user profile...")

        # Merge update data with existing profile
        current_profile_dict = user_to_update.profile.model_dump()
        update_payload_dict = profile_update_data.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)

        # Filter out fields that didn't change
        changed_fields = {k: v for k, v in update_payload_dict.items() if current_profile_dict.get(k) != v}
        if not changed_fields:
             log.info("No profile changes detected.")
             return user_to_update # Return original if no changes

        new_profile_data = {**current_profile_dict, **changed_fields}

        # Validate the merged profile data using the internal model
        try:
            validated_profile = UserProfile.model_validate(new_profile_data)
        except ValidationError as e:
            log.warning(f"Profile update validation failed: {e.errors()}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail=f"Invalid profile data: {e.errors()}")

        # Prepare update payload for repository
        update_internal = UserUpdateInternal(profile=validated_profile)

        # Call repository update
        updated_user = await user_repo.update(user_to_update.id, update_internal)
        if not updated_user:
            log.error("Failed to update user profile in repository.")
            # Log audit failure?
            await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="user_profile_update_failed",...)
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Failed to save profile updates.")

        log.success("User profile updated successfully.")
        # Log audit success
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
            action="user_profile_updated", status="success", entity_type="User",
            entity_id=user_to_update.id, audit_repo=None,
            details={"changes": changed_fields}, # Log only changed fields
            current_user=updater, request=None
        )
        return updated_user

    async def admin_update_user( # Separate function for admin actions
        self,
        user_to_update: UserInDB,
        admin_update_data: UserAdminUpdateAPI, # Specific API model
        admin_user: UserInDB, # Admin performing the action
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        audit_service: AuditService
    ) -> UserInDB:
        log = logger.bind(service="UserService", target_user_id=str(user_to_update.id), admin_id=str(admin_user.id))
        log.info("Service: Admin updating user roles/status...")

        update_payload = admin_update_data.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)
        if not update_payload:
             log.info("No admin update data provided.")
             return user_to_update

        # Prepare internal model for repo
        update_internal = UserUpdateInternal(**update_payload)

        updated_user = await user_repo.update(user_to_update.id, update_internal)
        if not updated_user:
            log.error("Failed to apply admin updates in repository.")
            await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="user_admin_update_failed",...)
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Failed to save admin updates.")

        log.success("Admin update successful.")
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
            action="user_admin_updated", status="success", entity_type="User",
            entity_id=user_to_update.id, audit_repo=None,
            details={"admin_changes": update_payload},
            current_user=admin_user, request=None
        )
        return updated_user

    # Modify adjust_balance to use the repo method and maybe trigger banking
    async def adjust_customer_balance( # Renamed from update_customer_balance for clarity
        self,
        user_id: ObjectId,
        amount_change_decimal: Decimal, # Expect Decimal here
        reason: str,
        actor: Optional[UserInDB], # User performing the change (or None for system)
        user_repo: UserRepository,
        audit_service: AuditService,
        # banking_service: BankingService, # Optionally trigger banking transaction?
        order_ref: Optional[str] = None
    ):
        """Adjusts customer balance using the repository method and logs."""
        log = logger.bind(service="UserService", user_id=str(user_id), change=str(amount_change_decimal), reason=reason)
        log.info("Service: Adjusting customer balance...")

        success = await user_repo.update_balance(user_id, amount_change_decimal) # Use repo method

        audit_status = "success" if success else "failure"
        error_msg = None if success else "Repository update failed"

        if not success:
             log.error("Failed to update balance via repository.")
             # Don't raise here, just log audit failure
        else:
             log.success("Customer balance adjusted successfully via repository.")

        # Always log the attempt
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
            action="customer_balance_adjusted", status=audit_status, entity_type="User",
            entity_id=user_id, audit_repo=None,
            details={"adjustment": str(amount_change_decimal), "reason": reason, "order_ref": order_ref},
            error_message=error_msg,
            current_user=actor, request=None
        )

        # Optionally: Create a corresponding Banking Transaction for adjustments?
        # if success and banking_service and amount_change_decimal != Decimal("0.00"):
        #     trx_type = "other_income" if amount_change_decimal > 0 else "other_expense"
        #     trx_internal = TransactionCreateInternal(type=trx_type, amount=abs(amount_change_decimal), ...)
        #     await banking_service.record_transaction(...)

        if not success:
            # Now raise exception after logging failure
            raise RuntimeError("Failed to update customer balance in database.")

# ... (get_user_service) ...

**3. Endpoints (Rotas)**

python
# app/modules/people/routers.py
# ... (imports: APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status, List, Optional, Path, Request, Body) ...
from .services import UserService, get_user_service
from .repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from .models import UserAPI, UserProfileAPI, UserCreateAdminAPI, UserProfileUpdateAPI, UserAdminUpdateAPI, AdjustBalancePayloadAPI # Import API models
from app.core.security import CurrentUser, UserInDB, require_role, oauth2_scheme # For /me
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service
from app.models.api_common import DetailResponse, StatusResponse # Common responses
from decimal import Decimal # For balance adjustment

auth_router = APIRouter() # Keep auth separate? Or merge into users_router? Keep separate for now.
users_router = APIRouter()

# --- /me Endpoint ---
@auth_router.get("/me", response_model=UserAPI, summary="Get current user details", tags=["Authentication"])
async def read_users_me(
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Uses get_current_active_user
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service) # For profile conversion
):
    """
    Returns the details of the currently authenticated user.
    """
    # UserInDB -> UserAPI conversion (Profile conversion happens here)
    # Exclude sensitive fields like hashed_password implicitly via UserAPI model
    profile_api = await user_service.get_user_profile_api(current_user)
    user_api_data = current_user.model_dump(exclude={'hashed_password', 'profile'})
    user_api_data['profile'] = profile_api
    user_api_data['id'] = str(user_api_data['id']) # Ensure ID is string

    return UserAPI.model_validate(user_api_data)


# --- User Profile CRUD ---

@users_router.get(
    "/me/profile",
    response_model=UserProfileAPI,
    summary="Get my profile",
    tags=["Users & People - Profile"]
)
async def get_my_profile_endpoint(
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service)
):
    """Retrieves the profile data for the currently logged-in user."""
    return await user_service.get_user_profile_api(current_user)

@users_router.patch(
    "/me/profile",
    response_model=UserProfileAPI,
    summary="Update my profile",
    tags=["Users & People - Profile"]
)
async def update_my_profile_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    profile_update: UserProfileUpdateAPI, # API model for payload
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository), # Needed by service
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service) # Needed by service
):
    """Updates the profile information for the currently logged-in user."""
    try:
        updated_user_db = await user_service.update_user_profile(
            user_to_update=current_user,
            profile_update_data=profile_update,
            updater=current_user, # User updates their own profile
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service
        )
        return await user_service.get_user_profile_api(updated_user_db)
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("Error updating own profile")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error updating profile.")


# --- Admin User Management ---

@users_router.post(
    "/",
    response_model=UserAPI,
    status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin"]))],
    summary="Create a new user (Admin)",
    tags=["Users & People - Admin"]
)
async def create_user_admin_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    user_in: UserCreateAdminAPI, # Specific admin create model
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin creating user
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository),
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service)
):
    """(Admin Only) Creates a new user with specified roles and profile."""
    try:
        # Prepare internal creation model
        profile_internal = UserProfile.model_validate(user_in.profile.model_dump()) if user_in.profile else UserProfile()
        user_create_internal = UserCreateInternal(
            email=user_in.email,
            hashed_password=user_in.password, # Service will hash
            profile=profile_internal,
            roles=user_in.roles or ["customer"],
            is_active=user_in.is_active
        )
        created_user_db = await user_service.create_user(
            user_data=user_create_internal,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            creator=current_user
        )
        # Convert to API response model
        profile_api = await user_service.get_user_profile_api(created_user_db)
        user_api_data = created_user_db.model_dump(exclude={'hashed_password', 'profile'})
        user_api_data['profile'] = profile_api
        user_api_data['id'] = str(user_api_data['id'])
        return UserAPI.model_validate(user_api_data)
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc # Propagate 409 Conflict etc.
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("Admin user creation failed.")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error creating user.")

@users_router.get(
    "/{user_id}",
    response_model=UserAPI,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "manager", "support"]))], # Who can view other users?
    summary="Get user details by ID (Admin)",
    tags=["Users & People - Admin"]
)
async def get_user_admin_endpoint(
    user_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the user to retrieve"),
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository)
):
    """(Admin/Staff Only) Retrieves full details for a specific user by ID."""
    user_db = await user_service.get_user_by_id(user_id, user_repo)
    if not user_db:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="User not found")

    # Convert to API response model
    profile_api = await user_service.get_user_profile_api(user_db)
    user_api_data = user_db.model_dump(exclude={'hashed_password', 'profile'})
    user_api_data['profile'] = profile_api
    user_api_data['id'] = str(user_api_data['id'])
    return UserAPI.model_validate(user_api_data)

@users_router.patch(
    "/{user_id}/profile",
    response_model=UserProfileAPI,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin"]))], # Only admin updates others' profiles?
    summary="Update user profile (Admin)",
    tags=["Users & People - Admin"]
)
async def update_user_profile_admin_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    user_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the user whose profile to update"),
    profile_update: UserProfileUpdateAPI,
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin performing action
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository),
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service)
):
    """(Admin Only) Updates profile information for a specific user."""
    user_to_update = await user_repo.get_by_id(user_id)
    if not user_to_update:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="User not found")

    try:
        updated_user_db = await user_service.update_user_profile(
            user_to_update=user_to_update,
            profile_update_data=profile_update,
            updater=current_user, # Log admin as updater
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service
        )
        return await user_service.get_user_profile_api(updated_user_db)
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Admin failed to update profile for user {user_id}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error updating profile.")


@users_router.patch(
    "/{user_id}/status",
    response_model=UserAPI,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin"]))],
    summary="Update user roles or active status (Admin)",
    tags=["Users & People - Admin"]
)
async def update_user_status_admin_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    user_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the user to update"),
    admin_update: UserAdminUpdateAPI, # Payload with roles/is_active
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin performing action
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository),
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service)
):
    """(Admin Only) Updates a user's roles or active status."""
    user_to_update = await user_repo.get_by_id(user_id)
    if not user_to_update:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="User not found")

    try:
        updated_user_db = await user_service.admin_update_user(
            user_to_update=user_to_update,
            admin_update_data=admin_update,
            admin_user=current_user,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service
        )
        # Convert to API response model
        profile_api = await user_service.get_user_profile_api(updated_user_db)
        user_api_data = updated_user_db.model_dump(exclude={'hashed_password', 'profile'})
        user_api_data['profile'] = profile_api
        user_api_data['id'] = str(user_api_data['id'])
        return UserAPI.model_validate(user_api_data)
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Admin failed to update status/roles for user {user_id}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error updating user status/roles.")


# --- Balance Adjustment Endpoint ---
@users_router.post(
    "/{user_id}/balance/adjust",
    response_model=CustomerBalanceResponseAPI, # Return new balance
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "finance"]))], # Who can adjust balance?
    summary="Adjust customer balance (Admin/Finance)",
    tags=["Users & People - Admin", "Finance"] # Add to Finance tag?
)
async def adjust_customer_balance_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    user_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the user whose balance to adjust"),
    payload: AdjustBalancePayloadAPI, # Amount and reason
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin/Finance user performing action
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository),
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service)
):
    """(Admin/Finance Only) Manually adjusts a customer's balance with a reason."""
    user_to_adjust = await user_repo.get_by_id(user_id)
    if not user_to_adjust:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="User not found")

    # Use the validated decimal amount from the payload model
    amount_decimal = payload._amount_decimal
    if amount_decimal is None: # Should be caught by Pydantic validation
         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid amount format.")

    try:
        # Service handles the update and audit logging
        await user_service.adjust_customer_balance(
            user_id=user_to_adjust.id,
            amount_change_decimal=amount_decimal,
            reason=payload.reason,
            actor=current_user,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            order_ref=payload.order_ref
        )
        # Fetch the updated balance to return
        new_balance_decimal = await user_service.get_customer_balance(user_id, user_repo)
        return CustomerBalanceResponseAPI(user_id=user_id, balance=str(new_balance_decimal))

    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        raise http_exc
    except (RuntimeError, Exception) as e:
        logger.exception(f"Error adjusting balance for user {user_id}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Internal server error adjusting balance: {e}")

**4. Intents (Dispatcher)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py
# ... (imports: logger, HTTPException, services, repos, models, UserInDB, etc.) ...
from app.modules.people.services import UserService, get_user_service
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from app.modules.people.models import UserAPI, UserProfileAPI, CustomerBalanceResponseAPI, UserProfileUpdateAPI # API Models
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service
from decimal import Decimal # For balance adjustment

# --- Action Functions ---

async def get_my_profile_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> UserAPI:
    """Action to get the profile of the current user."""
    log = logger.bind(intent="get_my_profile", user_id=str(user.id))
    log.info("Executing get_my_profile action...")
    # User object is already available from dispatcher
    # Convert to API model
    people_service: UserService = await get_people_service()
    profile_api = await people_service.get_user_profile_api(user)
    user_api_data = user.model_dump(exclude={'hashed_password', 'profile'})
    user_api_data['profile'] = profile_api
    user_api_data['id'] = str(user_api_data['id'])
    response_model = UserAPI.model_validate(user_api_data)
    return response_model.model_dump(mode='json') # Return dict

async def update_my_profile_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> UserProfileAPI:
    """Action to update parts of the current user's profile."""
    log = logger.bind(intent="update_my_profile", user_id=str(user.id))
    log.info("Executing update_my_profile action...")
    log.debug(f"Update payload: {payload}")

    # Validate payload against UserProfileUpdateAPI
    try:
        profile_update_api = UserProfileUpdateAPI.model_validate(payload)
    except ValidationError as e:
        log.warning(f"Validation failed for profile update: {e.errors()}")
        raise ValueError(f"Invalid profile update data: {e.errors()}")

    # Get dependencies
    people_service: UserService = await get_people_service()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()
    audit_service: AuditService = await get_audit_service()

    # Call service
    try:
        updated_user_db = await people_service.update_user_profile(
            user_to_update=user,
            profile_update_data=profile_update_api,
            updater=user, # User updates self
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service
        )
        updated_profile_api = await people_service.get_user_profile_api(updated_user_db)
        return updated_profile_api.model_dump(mode='json') # Return dict
    except HTTPException as e:
        raise # Re-raise HTTP exceptions from service
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception("Unexpected error during update_my_profile_action")
        raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to update profile: {e}") # Let dispatcher handle

async def adjust_user_balance_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> CustomerBalanceResponseAPI:
    """Action for an admin to adjust another user's balance."""
    log = logger.bind(intent="adjust_user_balance", admin_id=str(user.id))
    log.info("Executing adjust_user_balance action...")

    # Check if user has admin/finance role (Dispatcher should check this? Or service?)
    # Let's assume dispatcher passes only if user is admin/finance for this intent.
    if "admin" not in user.roles and "finance" not in user.roles:
         raise PermissionError("User does not have permission to adjust balance.")

    target_user_id_str = payload.get("user_identifier")
    amount_str = payload.get("amount")
    reason = payload.get("reason")
    order_ref = payload.get("order_ref")

    if not target_user_id_str or amount_str is None or not reason:
        raise ValueError("Missing target user, amount, or reason for balance adjustment.")

    # Validate amount
    try:
        amount_decimal = Decimal(amount_str).quantize(Decimal("0.01"))
    except InvalidOperation:
        raise ValueError("Invalid amount format for adjustment.")

    # Get dependencies
    people_service: UserService = await get_people_service()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()
    audit_service: AuditService = await get_audit_service()

    # Find target user
    target_user = await user_repo.get_by_id(target_user_id_str) # Assume identifier is ID for now
    if not target_user:
        raise ValueError(f"Target user '{target_user_id_str}' not found.")

    # Call service
    try:
        await people_service.adjust_customer_balance(
            user_id=target_user.id,
            amount_change_decimal=amount_decimal,
            reason=reason,
            actor=user, # Admin is the actor
            user_repo=user_repo,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            order_ref=order_ref
        )
        # Fetch and return new balance
        new_balance_decimal = await people_service.get_customer_balance(str(target_user.id), user_repo)
        response = CustomerBalanceResponseAPI(user_id=str(target_user.id), balance=str(new_balance_decimal))
        return response.model_dump(mode='json') # Return dict

    except HTTPException as e:
        raise # Re-raise HTTP exceptions
    except (RuntimeError, Exception) as e:
        log.exception(f"Failed to adjust balance for user {target_user_id_str}")
        raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to adjust balance: {e}")


# --- Update INTENT_ACTION_MAP ---
INTENT_ACTION_MAP: Dict[str, Callable[[Dict[str, Any], UserInDB], Awaitable[Any]]] = {
    # ... (intents: create_order, get_my_schedule, send_delivery_message, etc.) ...
    "get_my_profile": get_my_profile_action,
    "get_customer_balance": get_customer_balance_action, # Already added? Ensure it's correct.
    "update_my_profile": update_my_profile_action,
    "adjust_user_balance": adjust_user_balance_action, # Admin only
    # ...
}

from typing import Literal

```python
# Criar prompt para execução do Item 5: Transações com rollback e segurança (banking)

item_5_prompt = """
Você está atuando como engenheiro executor do sistema AgentOS da empresa VoulezVous.

Stack: FastAPI + MongoDB + estrutura modular (schemas, services, routes, repository). Toda funcionalidade importante se integra via dispatcher central no endpoint /process_request. O sistema já possui usuários com saldo e papéis. Os módulos `sales`, `delivery`, `scheduling` e `people` já fazem chamadas de transações internas.

---

### MISSÃO: Implementar o Item 5 do Roadmap Urgente

**Título:** Transações com rollback e segurança (banking)

---

### FUNCIONALIDADES:

1. **Modelo completo de transação**
   - Campos: `type`, `amount`, `currency`, `description`, `status`, `associated_user_id`, `associated_order_id`, `created_at`, `updated_at`
   - Tipos possíveis: `sale_income`, `shift_fee`, `refund`, `bonus`, `adjustment`, `correction`
   - Estados: `pending`, `completed`, `failed`, `cancelled`, `refunded`

2. **Criação e finalização de transações**
   - Serviço: `BankingService.record_transaction(...)`
     - Valida saldo se for débito
     - Atualiza saldo do usuário via `UserRepository.update_balance`
     - Salva transação com status `completed`
     - Gera auditoria com motivo
     - Transações `pending` podem ser confirmadas ou canceladas depois

3. **Rollback explícito**
   - Serviço: `BankingService.rollback_transaction(transaction_id)`
     - Reverte impacto no saldo
     - Marca transação como `cancelled` ou `refunded`
     - Registra nova transação de correção (`type=correction`)
     - Audita a reversão com o `actor`

4. **Endpoints REST**
   - `POST /transactions` → cria e finaliza transação
   - `POST /transactions/{id}/rollback` → faz rollback manual
   - `GET /transactions/{id}` → ver detalhes
   - `GET /users/{id}/transactions` → histórico de transações

5. **Intents no dispatcher**
   - `get_my_transactions`: retorna extrato do usuário logado
   - `get_transaction_status`: mostra status e descrição de uma transação
   - `request_refund`: dispara rollback de uma transação específica

---

### COMO ENTREGAR

Para cada funcionalidade:
- Gere os schemas (internal/API)
- Crie a lógica nos serviços com rollback auditável
- Adicione as rotas REST
- Mapeie intents no dispatcher
- Siga os padrões do AgentOS

Nada de explicações. Apenas entrega.
"""

# Salvar como arquivo para uso direto
prompt_path_item_5 = "/mnt/data/gemini_prompt_item_5_banking_transactions_rollback.txt"
with open(prompt_path_item_5, "w") as f:
    f.write(item_5_prompt)

prompt_path_item_5
```

**1. Schemas (Modelos de Dados)**

python
# app/modules/banking/models.py
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, ConfigDict, field_validator
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any, Literal
from datetime import datetime
from bson import ObjectId
from decimal import Decimal

from app.models.api_common import PyObjectId

# --- Constants ---
TRANSACTION_TYPES = Literal[
    "sale_income",        # Receita de venda
    "shift_fee",          # Débito pela alocação em turno (do saldo do usuário)
    "refund_outgoing",    # Reembolso enviado ao cliente (saída)
    "bonus_income",       # Bônus/Crédito para usuário (entrada)
    "manual_adjustment",  # Ajuste manual (entrada/saída) - feito por admin
    "correction",         # Transação criada para corrigir/reverter outra
    "payment_received",   # Pagamento recebido de cliente (aumenta saldo)
    "commission_payout",  # Pagamento de comissão (saída)
    "other_income",       # Outras receitas
    "other_expense"       # Outras despesas
]
TRANSACTION_STATUSES = Literal[
    "pending",            # Esperando confirmação externa (ex: pagamento)
    "completed",          # Concluída com sucesso e saldo atualizado
    "failed",             # Falhou (ex: pagamento recusado)
    "cancelled",          # Cancelada antes da conclusão
    "rolled_back",        # Revertida por uma transação de correção
    "pending_rollback"    # Reversão solicitada, aguardando processamento
]

# --- Internal/DB Models ---
class TransactionBase(BaseModel):
    transaction_ref: str = Field(..., unique=True)
    type: TRANSACTION_TYPES
    amount: Decimal # Always positive, use type to determine flow (income/expense)
    currency: str = Field(default="BRL", max_length=3)
    description: str
    status: TRANSACTION_STATUSES
    associated_user_id: Optional[ObjectId] = None # User whose balance is affected
    associated_order_id: Optional[ObjectId] = None # Optional link to order
    associated_shift_id: Optional[ObjectId] = None # Optional link to shift
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None # For extra info like gateway IDs

    @field_validator('amount')
    @classmethod
    def amount_must_be_positive(cls, v: Decimal) -> Decimal:
        if v < Decimal("0.00"):
            # Internal amount should always be positive; type determines direction.
            # Service layer ensures correct sign for balance adjustment.
            raise ValueError('Internal transaction amount must be positive.')
        return v.quantize(Decimal("0.01")) # Ensure 2 decimal places

class TransactionCreateInternal(TransactionBase):
    # Inherits fields, status defaults might be set by service
    status: TRANSACTION_STATUSES = "completed" # Default, service can override to pending

class TransactionUpdateInternal(BaseModel):
    # Fields allowed for update (mainly status)
    status: Optional[TRANSACTION_STATUSES] = None
    description: Optional[str] = None # Allow updating description?
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None # Allow adding metadata
    rollback_reason: Optional[str] = None # Store reason for rollback

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra='ignore')

class TransactionInDB(TransactionBase):
    id: PyObjectId = Field(..., alias="_id")
    rollback_reason: Optional[str] = None # Reason if rolled back
    rolled_back_by_trx_ref: Optional[str] = None # Link to correction transaction
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)

    model_config = ConfigDict(
        populate_by_name=True,
        arbitrary_types_allowed=True,
        json_encoders={ObjectId: str, datetime: lambda dt: dt.isoformat(), Decimal: str}
    )

# --- API Models ---
class TransactionAPI(BaseModel):
    id: str
    transaction_ref: str
    type: TRANSACTION_TYPES
    amount: str # Return as string
    currency: str
    description: str
    status: TRANSACTION_STATUSES
    associated_user_id: Optional[str] = None
    associated_order_id: Optional[str] = None
    associated_shift_id: Optional[str] = None
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    rollback_reason: Optional[str] = None
    rolled_back_by_trx_ref: Optional[str] = None
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime

    model_config = ConfigDict(from_attributes=True)

class TransactionCreateAPI(BaseModel): # For manual creation endpoint (Admin)
    type: TRANSACTION_TYPES
    amount_str: str = Field(..., alias="amount", description="Positive value of transaction. Type determines direction.")
    currency: str = Field(default="BRL")
    description: str
    status: Optional[TRANSACTION_STATUSES] = "completed" # Allow setting initial status?
    associated_user_id: Optional[str] = None
    associated_order_id: Optional[str] = None
    associated_shift_id: Optional[str] = None
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None

    _amount_decimal: Optional[Decimal] = None

    @field_validator('amount_str')
    @classmethod
    def validate_amount_str(cls, v: str) -> str:
        try:
            dec_val = Decimal(v).quantize(Decimal("0.01"))
            if dec_val <= Decimal("0.00"): # Amount must be positive for creation API
                 raise ValueError("Amount must be a positive number string.")
            cls._amount_decimal = dec_val
            return v
        except InvalidOperation:
            raise ValueError("Invalid amount format. Use string like '123.45'.")

class RollbackPayloadAPI(BaseModel):
    reason: str = Field(..., min_length=10, description="Mandatory reason for rollback")

**2. Lógica (Service & Repository)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/banking/repository.py (Modify/Add)**

python
# app/modules/banking/repository.py
# ... (imports: ObjectId, logger, Decimal, BaseRepository, models, etc) ...
from .models import TransactionInDB, TransactionCreateInternal, TransactionUpdateInternal

class TransactionRepository(BaseRepository[TransactionInDB, TransactionCreateInternal, TransactionUpdateInternal]):
    # ... (existing create_indexes, _prepare_data_for_db) ...

    async def get_by_ref(self, transaction_ref: str) -> Optional[TransactionInDB]:
        """Finds a transaction by its unique reference."""
        return await self.get_by({"transaction_ref": transaction_ref})

    async def list_by_user(
        self,
        user_id: ObjectId,
        start_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
        end_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 100
    ) -> List[TransactionInDB]:
        """Lists transactions for a specific user, optionally filtered by date."""
        query: Dict[str, Any] = {"associated_user_id": user_id}
        if start_date or end_date:
            query["created_at"] = {}
            if start_date: query["created_at"]["$gte"] = start_date
            if end_date: query["created_at"]["$lte"] = end_date # Adjust for end of day if needed

        # Most recent first
        return await self.list_by(query=query, skip=skip, limit=limit, sort=[("created_at", DESCENDING)])


# ... (get_transaction_repository) ...

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/banking/services.py (Modify/Add)**

python
# app/modules/banking/services.py
# ... (imports: Optional, List, Dict, Any, datetime, ObjectId, HTTPException, status, logger, Decimal) ...
from .repository import TransactionRepository
from .models import (
    TransactionInDB, TransactionCreateInternal, TransactionUpdateInternal,
    TRANSACTION_TYPES, TRANSACTION_STATUSES
)
from app.modules.people.services import UserService, get_user_service
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository
from app.modules.people.models import UserInDB
from app.core.counters import CounterService
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service

class BankingService:

    # --- Helper to determine balance change sign ---
    def _get_balance_change_sign(self, transaction_type: TRANSACTION_TYPES) -> int:
        # Positive means increase user balance (e.g., payment received, bonus)
        # Negative means decrease user balance (e.g., sale income, shift fee)
        if transaction_type in ["payment_received", "bonus_income", "other_income", "correction"]: # Correction sign depends on context
            return 1
        elif transaction_type in ["sale_income", "shift_fee", "refund_outgoing", "manual_adjustment", "commission_payout", "other_expense"]:
            return -1
        else:
            return 0 # Unknown type, no balance change? Or error?

    async def record_transaction(
        self,
        transaction_in: TransactionCreateInternal, # Expect internal model
        banking_repo: TransactionRepository,
        counter_service: CounterService,
        audit_service: AuditService,
        user_service: UserService, # <<< Need UserService for balance adjustments
        user_repo: UserRepository, # <<< Need UserRepo for balance adjustments
        actor: Optional[UserInDB] = None, # User performing action (or None for system)
        validate_balance: bool = True # <<< Flag to check balance before debit
    ) -> TransactionInDB:
        log = logger.bind(service="BankingService", type=transaction_in.type)
        log.info("Service: Recording transaction...")

        if transaction_in.amount <= Decimal("0.00"):
             raise ValueError("Transaction amount must be positive.")

        # 1. Determine Balance Impact
        balance_sign = self._get_balance_change_sign(transaction_in.type)
        balance_adjustment = transaction_in.amount * balance_sign

        target_user_id = transaction_in.associated_user_id

        # 2. Validate Balance (if debiting and required)
        if target_user_id and balance_adjustment < Decimal("0.00") and validate_balance:
            log.debug(f"Validating balance for user {target_user_id} before debit...")
            try:
                 current_balance = await user_service.get_customer_balance(str(target_user_id), user_repo)
                 if current_balance + balance_adjustment < Decimal("0.00"): # Check if sufficient balance
                      log.warning(f"Insufficient balance for user {target_user_id}. Needed: {-balance_adjustment}, Has: {current_balance}")
                      # Should we create transaction as failed or raise exception? Raise for now.
                      raise HTTPException(
                          status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT, # 409 Conflict seems appropriate
                          detail=f"Insufficient balance for user. Required: {-balance_adjustment:.2f}, Available: {current_balance:.2f}"
                      )
            except HTTPException as http_exc: # Catch 404 from get_customer_balance
                 log.error(f"Cannot validate balance: User {target_user_id} not found.")
                 raise http_exc # Re-raise 404
            except Exception as bal_e:
                 log.exception("Error validating user balance.")
                 raise RuntimeError(f"Error validating balance: {bal_e}")

        # 3. Generate Reference
        try:
            trx_ref = await counter_service.generate_reference("TRX")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Could not generate transaction reference")

        # 4. Prepare DB Data
        trx_data = transaction_in.model_dump()
        trx_data["transaction_ref"] = trx_ref
        # Ensure associated IDs are ObjectIds
        for key in ["associated_user_id", "associated_order_id", "associated_shift_id"]:
            if trx_data.get(key):
                 trx_data[key] = banking_repo._to_objectid(trx_data[key])

        # 5. Create Transaction in DB
        try:
            # Set initial status (default is completed, can be pending if needed)
            trx_data["status"] = transaction_in.status
            created_trx_db = await banking_repo.create(trx_data)
            log.success(f"Transaction {trx_ref} recorded successfully with status '{created_trx_db.status}'.")
        except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
            log.error(f"Failed to record transaction {trx_ref}: {e}")
            # Log audit failure?
            await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="transaction_record_failed", status="failure", ...)
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Could not record transaction: {e}")

        # 6. Update Balance (if transaction is completed and affects a user)
        balance_update_success = True
        if created_trx_db.status == "completed" and target_user_id and balance_adjustment != Decimal("0.00"):
            log.info(f"Updating balance for user {target_user_id} by {balance_adjustment} due to trx {trx_ref}")
            try:
                await user_service.adjust_customer_balance(
                    user_id=target_user_id,
                    amount_change_decimal=balance_adjustment,
                    reason=f"Transaction {trx_ref}: {created_trx_db.description}",
                    actor=actor,
                    user_repo=user_repo,
                    audit_service=audit_service,
                    order_ref=str(created_trx_db.associated_order_id) if created_trx_db.associated_order_id else None
                )
            except Exception as balance_e:
                log.error(f"Failed to update customer balance for completed transaction {trx_ref}: {balance_e}")
                balance_update_success = False
                # What to do if balance update fails AFTER transaction commit? Critical state.
                # Option 1: Mark transaction as 'failed_balance_update'?
                # Option 2: Attempt to schedule a retry for balance update?
                # Option 3: Raise critical alert for manual intervention.
                # For now, log error and continue, but mark flag.
                # TODO: Implement strategy for handling this inconsistency.
                # Mark transaction status as failed?
                await banking_repo.update(created_trx_db.id, {"status": "failed", "metadata.error": "Balance update failed post-commit"})


        # 7. Log Audit for Transaction Recording
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
             action="transaction_recorded", status="success", entity_type="Transaction",
             entity_id=created_trx_db.id, audit_repo=None,
             details=created_trx_db.model_dump(mode='json'),
             current_user=actor, request=None # Request is None as it's called from service
         )

        if not balance_update_success:
             # Raise error AFTER logging success for transaction creation but failure for balance
              raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Transaction {trx_ref} recorded, but failed to update associated user balance.")

        return created_trx_db

    async def rollback_transaction(
        self,
        transaction_id_str: str,
        reason: str,
        actor: UserInDB, # User performing the rollback
        banking_repo: TransactionRepository,
        counter_service: CounterService, # Needed for correction trx
        audit_service: AuditService,
        user_service: UserService,
        user_repo: UserRepository
    ) -> TransactionInDB: # Returns the original transaction, now marked rolled_back
        log = logger.bind(service="BankingService", target_trx_id=transaction_id_str, actor_id=str(actor.id))
        log.info("Service: Rolling back transaction...")

        original_trx = await banking_repo.get_by_id(transaction_id_str)
        if not original_trx:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="Transaction to rollback not found.")

        # 1. Check if already rolled back or not completed
        if original_trx.status == "rolled_back":
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail="Transaction has already been rolled back.")
        if original_trx.status not in ["completed", "failed"]: # Can rollback failed balance updates? Or only completed? Allow completed for now.
            raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail=f"Cannot rollback transaction with status '{original_trx.status}'.")

        # 2. Calculate Balance Reversal
        original_balance_sign = self._get_balance_change_sign(original_trx.type)
        balance_reversal_amount = original_trx.amount * original_balance_sign * -1 # Reverse the original adjustment

        # 3. Create Correction Transaction (Optional but good practice)
        correction_trx: Optional[TransactionInDB] = None
        if balance_reversal_amount != Decimal("0.00") and original_trx.associated_user_id:
            log.info(f"Creating correction transaction for rollback of {original_trx.transaction_ref}...")
            correction_type = "correction" # Or more specific like 'rollback_correction'
            correction_create = TransactionCreateInternal(
                type=correction_type,
                amount=abs(balance_reversal_amount), # Amount is always positive
                currency=original_trx.currency,
                description=f"Correction for rollback of Trx: {original_trx.transaction_ref}. Reason: {reason}",
                status="completed", # Correction is completed immediately
                associated_user_id=original_trx.associated_user_id,
                # Link correction back? Add field: correction_for_trx_ref ?
                metadata={"correction_for_trx_ref": original_trx.transaction_ref}
            )
            # Call record_transaction recursively? Careful with infinite loops.
            # Better to have a dedicated internal creation method or call repo directly?
            # Call record_transaction BUT disable balance validation for the correction.
            try:
                correction_trx = await self.record_transaction(
                    transaction_in=correction_create,
                    banking_repo=banking_repo,
                    counter_service=counter_service,
                    audit_service=audit_service,
                    user_service=user_service,
                    user_repo=user_repo,
                    actor=actor, # Log actor for correction
                    validate_balance=False # Don't validate balance for correction itself (it might be fixing insufficient funds)
                )
                log.info(f"Correction transaction {correction_trx.transaction_ref} created.")
            except Exception as corr_e:
                log.error(f"Failed to create correction transaction during rollback: {corr_e}")
                # Should we halt the rollback? Yes, probably.
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Failed to create correction transaction: {corr_e}")


        # 4. Update Original Transaction Status
        log.info(f"Updating original transaction {original_trx.transaction_ref} status to rolled_back.")
        update_data = TransactionUpdateInternal(
            status="rolled_back",
            rollback_reason=reason,
            # metadata updates if needed
        )
        if correction_trx:
             # Add link to the correction transaction
              update_data.rolled_back_by_trx_ref = correction_trx.transaction_ref

        updated_original_trx = await banking_repo.update(original_trx.id, update_data)
        if not updated_original_trx:
            log.critical(f"CRITICAL: Failed to mark original transaction {original_trx.id} as rolled_back AFTER balance reversal/correction! Manual check needed.")
            # TODO: Alert admin
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Failed to finalize rollback status update.")

        log.success(f"Transaction {original_trx.transaction_ref} successfully rolled back.")
        # 5. Log Audit for Rollback Action
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
             action="transaction_rolled_back", status="success", entity_type="Transaction",
             entity_id=original_trx.id, audit_repo=None,
             details={"reason": reason, "correction_trx_ref": correction_trx.transaction_ref if correction_trx else None},
             current_user=actor, request=None
         )

        return updated_original_trx # Return the original transaction with updated status


    async def get_transaction(self, transaction_id_str: str, banking_repo: TransactionRepository) -> Optional[TransactionInDB]:
         """Gets a single transaction by ID or Ref."""
         trx = await banking_repo.get_by_id(transaction_id_str)
         if not trx:
              trx = await banking_repo.get_by_ref(transaction_id_str) # Allow fetch by ref too
         return trx

    async def list_transactions_for_user(
        self,
        user_id_str: str,
        banking_repo: TransactionRepository,
        start_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
        end_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 100
    ) -> List[TransactionInDB]:
        """Lists transactions for a specific user."""
        user_objid = banking_repo._to_objectid(user_id_str)
        if not user_objid:
             raise ValueError("Invalid user_id format")
        return await banking_repo.list_by_user(user_objid, start_date, end_date, skip, limit)


# ... (get_banking_service) ...

# Add necessary imports
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation
from .models import TransactionCreateInternal # Assume internal model uses Decimal

**3. Endpoints (Rotas)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/banking/routers.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/banking/routers.py
# ... (imports: APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status, Query, Path, Request, List, Optional, datetime) ...
from .services import BankingService, get_banking_service
from .repository import TransactionRepository, get_transaction_repository
from .models import TransactionAPI, TransactionCreateAPI, RollbackPayloadAPI, TRANSACTION_TYPES, TRANSACTION_STATUSES # API Models
from app.core.security import CurrentUser, UserInDB, require_role
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service
from app.core.counters import CounterService, get_counter_service # For create
from app.modules.people.services import UserService, get_user_service # For create/rollback
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository # For create/rollback

banking_router = APIRouter()

# --- Helper ---
async def get_transaction_or_404(
    transaction_id: str = Path(..., description="ID or Ref of the Transaction"),
    banking_service: BankingService = Depends(get_banking_service),
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = Depends(get_transaction_repository) # Needed by service
) -> TransactionInDB:
    trx = await banking_service.get_transaction(transaction_id, banking_repo)
    if not trx:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="Transaction not found")
    return trx

# --- Endpoints ---

# POST /transactions (Manual Creation - Admin/Finance)
@banking_router.post(
    "/",
    response_model=TransactionAPI,
    status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "finance"]))],
    summary="Manually record a financial transaction",
    tags=["Banking"]
)
async def record_manual_transaction_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    transaction_in: TransactionCreateAPI, # API model for input
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin/Finance user
    banking_service: BankingService = Depends(get_banking_service),
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = Depends(get_transaction_repository),
    counter_service: CounterService = Depends(get_counter_service),
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service),
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service),
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository)
):
    """(Admin/Finance Only) Manually records a financial transaction and updates balance."""
    log = logger.bind(user_id=str(current_user.id))
    log.info(f"Endpoint: Manual transaction recording type '{transaction_in.type}'...")
    try:
        # Prepare internal model for service
        amount_dec = transaction_in._amount_decimal # Get validated decimal
        if amount_dec is None: raise HTTPException(400, "Invalid amount") # Should be caught earlier

        trx_internal = TransactionCreateInternal(
            type=transaction_in.type,
            amount=amount_dec, # Pass decimal to internal model
            currency=transaction_in.currency,
            description=transaction_in.description,
            status=transaction_in.status or "completed",
            associated_user_id=transaction_in.associated_user_id, # Pass as string, service converts
            associated_order_id=transaction_in.associated_order_id,
            associated_shift_id=transaction_in.associated_shift_id,
            metadata=transaction_in.metadata
        )

        # Service handles creation, balance validation/update, audit
        created_db = await banking_service.record_transaction(
            transaction_in=trx_internal,
            banking_repo=banking_repo,
            counter_service=counter_service,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            user_service=user_service,
            user_repo=user_repo,
            actor=current_user,
            validate_balance=True # Validate balance for manual debits
        )
        # Convert DB model back to API model
        return TransactionAPI.model_validate(created_db)

    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        # Log audit failure? Service might handle it for known errors like insufficient balance
        if http_exc.status_code != 409: # Avoid double logging insufficient balance
             await audit_service.log_audit_event(
                 action="manual_transaction_failed", status="failure", entity_type="Transaction",
                 error_message=http_exc.detail, details=transaction_in.model_dump(),
                 current_user=current_user, request=request, audit_repo=None
             )
        raise http_exc
    except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
         await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="manual_transaction_failed", status="failure", ...)
         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e)) # Value errors likely 400
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception("Manual transaction recording failed.")
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="manual_transaction_failed", status="failure", ...)
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error recording transaction.")


# POST /transactions/{id}/rollback (Admin/Finance)
@banking_router.post(
    "/{transaction_id}/rollback",
    response_model=TransactionAPI, # Return the original transaction (now rolled back)
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "finance"]))],
    summary="Rollback a transaction",
    tags=["Banking"]
)
async def rollback_transaction_endpoint(
    request: Request,
    payload: RollbackPayloadAPI, # Reason for rollback
    original_trx: TransactionInDB = Depends(get_transaction_or_404), # Get original or 404
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(), # Admin/Finance user
    banking_service: BankingService = Depends(get_banking_service),
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = Depends(get_transaction_repository), # Pass to service
    counter_service: CounterService = Depends(get_counter_service), # Pass to service
    audit_service: AuditService = Depends(get_audit_service), # Pass to service
    user_service: UserService = Depends(get_user_service), # Pass to service
    user_repo: UserRepository = Depends(get_user_repository) # Pass to service
):
    """(Admin/Finance Only) Rolls back a completed transaction, adjusting balance and logging."""
    log = logger.bind(user_id=str(current_user.id), target_trx_id=str(original_trx.id))
    log.info(f"Endpoint: Rolling back transaction {original_trx.transaction_ref}...")
    try:
        # Service handles rollback logic, balance reversal, correction trx, audit
        rolled_back_trx_db = await banking_service.rollback_transaction(
            transaction_id_str=str(original_trx.id), # Pass ID string
            reason=payload.reason,
            actor=current_user,
            banking_repo=banking_repo,
            counter_service=counter_service,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            user_service=user_service,
            user_repo=user_repo
        )
        # Convert rolled-back original transaction to API model
        return TransactionAPI.model_validate(rolled_back_trx_db)

    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        # Service might raise 400 if already rolled back or wrong status
        # Audit handled by service
        raise http_exc
    except (ValueError, RuntimeError) as e:
        # Audit handled by service? Or log here? Log here for safety.
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(
             action="transaction_rollback_failed", status="failure", entity_type="Transaction",
             entity_id=original_trx.id, error_message=str(e), details={"reason": payload.reason},
             current_user=current_user, request=request, audit_repo=None
         )
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e)) # Likely 400
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception(f"Rollback failed for transaction {original_trx.transaction_ref}")
        await audit_service.log_audit_event(action="transaction_rollback_failed", status="failure", ...)
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error rolling back transaction.")


# GET /transactions/{id} (Admin/Finance/Support?)
@banking_router.get(
    "/{transaction_id}",
    response_model=TransactionAPI,
    dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "finance", "support"]))], # Adjust roles as needed
    summary="Get transaction details",
    tags=["Banking"]
)
async def get_transaction_endpoint(
    trx: TransactionInDB = Depends(get_transaction_or_404) # Use helper
):
    """Retrieves details for a specific financial transaction by ID or Ref."""
    # Helper already fetches the TransactionInDB object
    return TransactionAPI.model_validate(trx)


# GET /users/{user_id}/transactions (Admin/Finance/Support OR User themselves?)
@banking_router.get(
    "/users/{user_id}/transactions",
    response_model=List[TransactionAPI],
    # Permission check: Allow admin/finance OR the user themselves to see their own history
    # dependencies=[Depends(require_role(["admin", "finance", "support"]))], # Too broad?
    summary="List transactions for a specific user",
    tags=["Banking", "Users & People"] # Add to Users tag too?
)
async def list_user_transactions_endpoint(
    user_id: str = Path(..., description="ID of the user"),
    start_date: Optional[datetime] = Query(None),
    end_date: Optional[datetime] = Query(None),
    skip: int = Query(0, ge=0),
    limit: int = Query(100, ge=1, le=500),
    current_user: CurrentUser = Depends(),
    banking_service: BankingService = Depends(get_banking_service),
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = Depends(get_transaction_repository)
):
    """Retrieves the transaction history for a specific user."""
    # Permission Check
    if str(current_user.id) != user_id and not any(role in current_user.roles for role in ["admin", "finance", "support"]):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized to view this user's transactions.")

    try:
        transactions_db = await banking_service.list_transactions_for_user(
            user_id_str=user_id,
            banking_repo=banking_repo,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            skip=skip,
            limit=limit
        )
        return [TransactionAPI.model_validate(trx) for trx in transactions_db]
    except ValueError as ve: # Invalid user_id format from service
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(ve))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Error listing transactions for user {user_id}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error listing transactions.")

# Add other banking endpoints if needed (e.g., confirm/cancel pending)
# Remember to include banking_router in app/api/v1.py

**4. Intents (Dispatcher)**

**Arquivo: backend/app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py (Modificar/Adicionar)**

python
# app/modules/gateway/dispatcher.py
# ... (imports: logger, HTTPException, services, repos, models, UserInDB, etc.) ...
from app.modules.banking.services import BankingService, get_banking_service
from app.modules.banking.repository import TransactionRepository, get_transaction_repository
from app.modules.banking.models import TransactionAPI # API Model
from app.modules.people.repository import UserRepository, get_user_repository # Needed for rollback actor
from app.core.counters import CounterService, get_counter_service # Needed for rollback
from app.modules.office.services_audit import AuditService, get_audit_service # Needed for rollback
from app.modules.people.services import UserService, get_user_service # Needed for rollback


# --- Action Functions ---

async def get_my_transactions_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> List[TransactionAPI]:
    """Action to get the transaction history for the current user."""
    log = logger.bind(intent="get_my_transactions", user_id=str(user.id))
    log.info("Executing get_my_transactions action...")

    # Extract optional date filters from payload if provided by LLM
    start_date = payload.get("start_date") # Expect YYYY-MM-DD string? Needs parsing
    end_date = payload.get("end_date")
    limit = payload.get("limit", 20) # Limit results for chat view

    # Parse dates
    dt_start = datetime.fromisoformat(start_date) if start_date else None
    dt_end = datetime.fromisoformat(end_date) if end_date else None

    banking_service: BankingService = await get_banking_service()
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = await get_transaction_repository()

    transactions_db = await banking_service.list_transactions_for_user(
        user_id_str=str(user.id),
        banking_repo=banking_repo,
        start_date=dt_start,
        end_date=dt_end,
        limit=limit
    )
    # Convert to list of dicts for dispatcher return
    return [TransactionAPI.model_validate(t).model_dump(mode='json') for t in transactions_db]

async def get_transaction_status_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> Optional[TransactionAPI]:
    """Action to get the status and details of a specific transaction."""
    trx_identifier = payload.get("transaction_identifier") # ID or Ref
    if not trx_identifier:
        raise ValueError("Missing transaction identifier (ID or Ref).")

    log = logger.bind(intent="get_transaction_status", user_id=str(user.id), trx_id=trx_identifier)
    log.info("Executing get_transaction_status action...")

    banking_service: BankingService = await get_banking_service()
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = await get_transaction_repository()

    trx_db = await banking_service.get_transaction(trx_identifier, banking_repo)
    if not trx_db:
        raise ValueError(f"Transaction '{trx_identifier}' not found.")

    # Permission Check: Can anyone query any transaction status via LLM? Or only own/admin?
    # Add check here if needed:
    # if trx_db.associated_user_id != user.id and "admin" not in user.roles:
    #     raise PermissionError("Not authorized to view this transaction status.")

    # Convert to dict for dispatcher return
    return TransactionAPI.model_validate(trx_db).model_dump(mode='json')

async def request_refund_action(payload: dict, user: UserInDB) -> TransactionAPI:
    """Action to request a rollback/refund for a specific transaction."""
    trx_identifier = payload.get("transaction_identifier") # ID or Ref of transaction TO BE REFUNDED
    reason = payload.get("reason", "Refund requested via Advisor") # Reason might come from LLM

    if not trx_identifier:
        raise ValueError("Missing transaction identifier for refund request.")

    log = logger.bind(intent="request_refund", user_id=str(user.id), target_trx=trx_identifier)
    log.info("Executing request_refund action...")

    # Permission Check: Who can request refunds? Admin/Finance? The user associated?
    # For now, assume Admin/Finance role is needed (can be adjusted)
    if "admin" not in user.roles and "finance" not in user.roles:
         raise PermissionError("User does not have permission to request refunds/rollbacks.")

    # Get dependencies for rollback service call
    banking_service: BankingService = await get_banking_service()
    banking_repo: TransactionRepository = await get_transaction_repository()
    counter_service: CounterService = await get_counter_service()
    audit_service: AuditService = await get_audit_service()
    user_service: UserService = await get_user_service()
    user_repo: UserRepository = await get_user_repository()

    # Call the rollback service
    # Service needs ID string
    # Fetch the transaction first to pass to service? No, service fetches.
    try:
        # Note: get_transaction used transaction_id_str which is ID or Ref
        rolled_back_trx_db = await banking_service.rollback_transaction(
            transaction_id_str=trx_identifier,
            reason=reason,
            actor=user, # Admin user is the actor
            banking_repo=banking_repo,
            counter_service=counter_service,
            audit_service=audit_service,
            user_service=user_service,
            user_repo=user_repo
        )
        # Return the original transaction (now rolled back) as dict
        return TransactionAPI.model_validate(rolled_back_trx_db).model_dump(mode='json')
    except HTTPException as http_exc:
        # Convert HTTP exceptions from service to ValueError for dispatcher
        raise ValueError(f"Refund request failed: {http_exc.detail}")
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception(f"Unexpected error during refund request for {trx_identifier}")
        raise RuntimeError(f"Internal error processing refund: {e}")


# --- Update INTENT_ACTION_MAP ---
INTENT_ACTION_MAP: Dict[str, Callable[[Dict[str, Any], UserInDB], Awaitable[Any]]] = {
    # ... (intents: create_order, get_my_schedule, send_delivery_message, etc.) ...
    "get_my_transactions": get_my_transactions_action,
    "get_transaction_status": get_transaction_status_action,
    "request_refund": request_refund_action,
    "rollback_transaction": request_refund_action, # Alias
    # ...
}

# Ensure necessary imports like datetime, List, Decimal, TransactionAPI are present
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List
from decimal import Decimal
from app.modules.banking.models import TransactionAPI

## Response:
Claro. Aqui está o **prompt revisado e mais específico para o Gemini**, com instruções claras, diretas e operacionais — ideal para rodar o LLM Gateway da VoulezVous com precisão:

* * *

### **PROMPT PARA GEMINI (LLM Gateway da VoulezVous)**

Você é o cérebro operacional da empresa **VoulezVous**, atuando como **LLM Gateway do sistema AgentOS**. Seu papel é interpretar comandos de linguagem natural dos usuários e executar corretamente as ações correspondentes no backend da empresa.

**Contexto técnico:**

*   O backend está implementado em **FastAPI**, com serviços modulares como:
    
    *   `sales` (pedidos)
        
    *   `delivery` (entregas e chat com estafetas)
        
    *   `people` (usuários, perfis e saldo)
        
    *   `scheduling` (turnos e escala)
        
    *   `banking` (transações e rollback)
        
    *   `finance`, `office` (configuração e controle)
        
*   Existe um endpoint único de entrada: `POST /process_request`, que recebe **`{intent, entities}`** e aciona o serviço correto.
    

* * *

### **Sua Função Como Gateway de IA:**

Quando receber uma frase do usuário, você deve:

1.  **Identificar a `intent`** (ação que o usuário quer realizar).  
    Exemplo: `"Quero pedir 2 cafés"` → `create_order`
    
2.  **Extrair e estruturar as `entities`** em formato JSON, conforme os schemas definidos no backend.  
    Exemplo:
    
    ```json
    {
      "items": [
        { "product_identifier": "café", "quantity": 2 }
      ],
      "channel": "advisor"
    }
    ```
    
3.  **Retornar ao sistema:**
    
    *   `intent`: o nome da ação (string)
        
    *   `entities`: o payload validado (JSON)
        
    *   `natural_response`: uma resposta clara e simpática para o usuário com base no resultado
        

* * *

### **Regras e Restrições:**

*   **NÃO invente endpoints.** Use apenas as intents disponíveis:
    
    *   `create_order`
        
    *   `get_customer_balance`
        
    *   `get_my_schedule`
        
    *   `create_auto_shift`
        
    *   `send_delivery_message`
        
    *   `get_delivery_chat`
        
    *   `get_delivery_location`
        
    *   `update_my_profile`
        
    *   `adjust_user_balance`
        
    *   `get_my_transactions`
        
    *   `get_transaction_status`
        
    *   `request_refund`
        
*   **Sempre responda com o seguinte JSON de saída:**
    
    ```json
    {
      "intent": "nome_da_intent",
      "entities": { ... },
      "natural_response": "Texto amigável para o usuário"
    }
    ```
    
*   Se faltar informação essencial para executar, **peça ao usuário com clareza e contexto** (como um bom atendente faria).
    

* * *

### **Exemplo de Entrada e Saída:**

**Entrada do usuário:**

> "Quero marcar um turno amanhã das 9h às 18h com função motorista"

**Resposta sua:**

```json
{
  "intent": "create_auto_shift",
  "entities": {
    "shift_date": "2025-05-02",
    "start_time": "09:00",
    "end_time": "18:00",
    "required_role": "motorista",
    "max_participants": 1,
    "required_balance": "0.00"
  },
  "natural_response": "Turno solicitado com sucesso para amanhã das 9h às 18h com a função de motorista. Aguardando confirmação!"
}
```

* * *

### **Agora você está online. Receba a próxima instrução do usuário e processe.**

```txt
Você é um engenheiro responsável por completar o backend do sistema AgentOS/VoulezVous. O sistema já está majoritariamente pronto, com módulos em FastAPI, MongoDB (via Motor), autenticação, intents com LLM e orquestração centralizada via dispatcher.

Sua tarefa: **entregar apenas o que ainda falta** para o sistema funcionar de forma completa e operacional.

---

Módulos e funcionalidades que ainda precisam ser entregues:

1. [office]
  - CRUD completo de `/settings` e `/features` (nome, valor, tipo).
  - Auditoria (`/audit`): endpoint com filtros por entidade, ação, status, user_id, e período.
  - Repositório, modelos, serviços e permissões (admin-only).

2. [finance]
  - API consolidada para dashboard: fluxo de caixa, totais por tipo (receitas, despesas, comissões).
  - Cálculo de saldo real e saldo previsto.
  - Integração com transações e agendamentos.

3. [worker / fallback]
  - Celery task para entregas sem localização recente (`check_location_fallback`).
  - Task para preencher turnos com autoassign após X minutos se ainda estiverem vazios.
  - Envio de alerta via WebSocket para painel administrativo.

4. [observabilidade]
  - `GET /healthcheck`: status de MongoDB, Celery e uptime.
  - `GET /metrics`: contadores simples (pedidos hoje, saldo total, usuários ativos).

5. [segurança]
  - Middleware de rate limiting (por IP ou token).
  - Escopo de token para intents sensíveis: rollback, ajuste de saldo, ver transações.

6. [testes]
  - Testes automatizados com Pytest para:
    - Criação de pedidos e fallback de estoque
    - Tracking de entregas e chat entre cliente e estafeta
    - Transações com rollback e ajuste de saldo
  - Simulação de intent no dispatcher (via mock de LLM)

7. [infra/deploy]
  - Validar `Dockerfile`, `.env.example`, `pyproject.toml` e `start.sh`.
  - Garantir build automático, healthcheck, readiness para produção (Railway ou equivalente).

---

Requisitos:
- Use FastAPI + Motor (MongoDB async).
- Pydantic v2.
- Estrutura modular já está definida, siga os padrões existentes.
- Organize por arquivos e caminhos corretos (`backend/app/modules/...`).
- Não reescreva nada do que já está implementado.
- Código pronto para ser plugado direto.

Entregue apenas o código que falta para a plataforma VoulezVous funcionar de ponta a ponta.
```
